    17. Wɔka daa kyerɛ hɔn a wommbu me bi dɛ, EWURADZE na ɔse, Hom benya asomdwee; na obiara a ɔnantsew noara n'akoma ne ntsintsiman mu no so wɔse no dɛ, Mbusu bi nnkɛba hom do.
    18. Na woana na oegyina EWURADZE n'egyinamu, ama oeehu na ɔaatse n'asɛm? Woana na woetsie n'asɛm, ama wɔaapaa mu aka?
    19. Hwɛ, EWURADZE n'ehum, mekyerɛ n'ebufuhyew no, efir edzi, nyew, ekyinehyia ehum a ɔbɔbɔ ebesi emumuyɛfo etsifi a.
    20. EWURADZE n'ebufuw rennsan n'ekyir, ma ekodu dɛ obowie na ɔayɛ dza ɔahyehyɛ wɔ n'akoma mu nyina: nda a odzi ekyir no mu na hom bɛtse ase kofee.
    21. Nnyɛ emi mosomaa nkɔnhyɛfo no, naaso wotuu mbirika: emi mankasa annkyerɛ hɔn, naaso wɔhyɛɛ nkɔm.
    22. Na sɛ wogyinaa m'egyinatu mu a, nkyɛ wɔmaa me man tsiee me nsɛm, na wɔsaan hɔn fii hɔn kwan bɔn na hɔn ndzeyɛɛ bɔn no ho.
    23. Aso meyɛ Nyankopɔn a ɔbɛn, EWURADZE na ɔse, na nnyɛ Nyankopɔn a ɔwɔ ekyirekyir?
    24. Aso obi botum ehuntsa noho wɔ huntsabea bi a emi murunnhu no? EWURADZE na ɔse. Ana mennhyɛ ɔsor na asaase ma? EWURADZE na ɔse.
    25. Matse dza nkɔnhyɛfo a wɔhyɛ ator nkɔm wɔ me dzin mu aka, dɛ, Maso daa, maso daa.
    26. Ɔnkyɛr nkodu dabɛn ara na iyi bɔko nkɔnhyɛfo a wɔhyɛ ator nkɔm no akoma mu; nkɔnhyɛfo a wɔhyɛ hɔnankasa hɔn akoma mu ndaadaa nkɔm no a?
    27. Wɔdwen dɛ wɔbɛma me man werɛ efir me dzin wɔ hɔn adaaso a hɔn mu nyimpa biara ka kyerɛ ne nyɛnko no ntsi, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn egyanom werɛ fiir me dzin wɔ Baal ntsi no.
    28. Nkɔnhyɛnyi a ɔwɔ adaaso bi, ma ɔnka n'adaaso; na nyia ɔwɔ m'asɛm, ma ɔnka m'asɛm nokwar mu. Ebɛn na ntsɛw nye ewifua wɔ yɛ? EWURADZE na ɔse.
    29. Ana m'asɛm nntse dɛ ogya? EWURADZE na ɔse; na dɛ hamɛr a opuepue ɔbotan mu esinesin?
    30. Dɛm ntsi hwɛ, menye nkɔnhyɛfo no enya, EWURADZE na ɔse, hɔn a wowiawia m'asɛm wɔ hɔn nsɛfo nkyɛn no.
    31. Hwɛ, EWURADZE na ɔse, menye nkɔnhyɛfo a wɔdze hɔn tɛkyerɛma ka dɛ, Ɔno na ɔse, no enya.
    32. Hwɛ, menye hɔn a wɔhyɛ ator adaa ho nkɔm no enya, EWURADZE na ɔse, na wɔkeka kyerɛ, na wɔdze hɔn atorsɛm na hɔn ntuw hun ma me man wɔfom: naaso mannsoma hɔn, eso mannhyɛ hɔn; eso wɔrennyɛ mfaso bi mma ɔman yi koraa, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    33. Na sɛ ɔman yi, anaa nkɔnhyɛnyi no, anaa ɔsɔfo bi bisa wo dɛ, EWURADZE adzesoa nye bɛn a? Ɔno se hɔn dɛ, Adzesoa bɛn a? Mobɔtow hom egu, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    34. Na nkɔnhyɛnyi, na ɔsɔfo, na ɔman a wɔbɛka dɛ, EWURADZE n'adzesoa no, dze, mebɛtsea nyimpa no na ne fi mpo.
    35. Mbrɛ hom mu obiara nka nkyerɛ ne nyɛnko, na obiara nka nkyerɛ no nua nye yi, Ebɛnadze na EWURADZE ebua? Na, ebɛn asɛm na EWURADZE aka?
    36. Na EWURADZE adzesoa no dze, mma hom mmbɔ dzin bio, na obiara noara n'asɛm bɛdan no adzesoa; osiandɛ hom esi tseasefo Nyankopɔn, dɔm EWURADZE, hɛn Nyankopɔn no ne nsɛm tsir adze.
    37. Dɛm na hom nse nkɔnhyɛnyi no, Ebɛn na EWURADZE dze ebua wo? Asɛm bɛn na EWURADZE aka?
    38. Na sɛ hom se dɛ, EWURADZE n'adzesoa a; dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Osiandɛ hom ka asɛm yi, dɛ, EWURADZE n'adzesoa, na emi na masoma wɔ hom nkyɛn, dɛ, Mma hom nnka dɛ, EWURADZE n'adzesoa;
    39. dɛm ntsi, hwɛ, mo werɛ befir hom korakora, na matow hom na kurow a medze maa hom na hom egyanom no efi m'enyim akyen:
    40. na medze daa ahorohoraa, na daa enyito a werɛ nnkefir da, mebɛba hom do.

    Tsir 24

    1. EWURADZE dze kyerɛɛ me, na, hwɛ, adɔmba nkɛntsɛn sisi EWURADZE n'asɔrdan enyim; ofitsi ber a Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar nyaa Judahen Jehoiakim ne ba Jekonia, na Juda mbapɔmba na edwimfo, na atomfo fii Jerusalɛm, na ɔdze hɔn kɔr Babilɔn ndɔmmum ekyir no.
    2. Kɛntsɛn kor mu wɔ adɔmba a oye dɛ biribi, dɛ adɔmba a oedzi kan aber: na kɛntsɛn kor no so mu wɔ adɔmba a omuo dɛ biribi a wodzi a ɔnnyɛ yie, omuo dodow.
    3. Nna EWURADZE see me dɛ, Jeremia, ihu ebɛn? Na mesee dɛ, Adɔmba a; adɔmba papa no, oye dodow; na dza omuo no, omuo dodow ma wodzi a ɔnnyɛ, omuo koraa.
    4. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa me nkyɛn, dɛ, JER.24.5, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Israel Nyankopɔn no se nye yi; Mbrɛ adɔmba papa yi tse no, dɛmara so na mubobu Juda ndɔmmumfo a memaa wofii bea yi do kɔr Kaldeafo asaase no do no bi, mama hɔn yie.
    5. Na medze m'enyi mibesi hɔn do wɔ yie ntsi, na medze hɔn aba asaase yi do bio: na medze hɔn mibesisi hɔ, na murunndwuruw hɔn; na mebɛtsɛw hɔn, na murunntutu hɔn.
    6. Na mebɛma hɔn akoma ma wɔdze ehu me, dɛ emi nye EWURADZE: na wɔbɛyɛ me man, na mayɛ hɔn Nyankopɔn: na wɔdze hɔn akoma nyina bɛsan aba me nkyɛn.
    7. Na dɛ mbrɛ adɔmba a omuo a wodzi a ɔnnyɛ tse no, womuo dodow; ampaara mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Dɛmara na mibeyi Judahen Jedekia, na ne mbapɔmba, na Jerusalɛm nkaa a wɔaka asaase no do, na hɔn a wɔtse Egypt asaase do mama:
    8. mpo mibeyi hɔn mama ma wɔatow hɔn edzi akɔnaaba wɔ asaase do nhenman nyina mu ayɛ hɔn mbusu; ma wɔayɛ ahorohoraa na kasabɛbu, asesardze na ndom, wɔ mbeambea nyina a mebɛpam hɔn makɔ nyinara.
    9. Na mobɔsoma afona, na ɔkɔm, na ɔyardɔm wɔ hɔn mu, ma ekesi dɛ wɔbɛsa koraa wɔ asaase a medze maa hɔn na hɔn egyanom no do.

    Tsir 25

    1. Asɛm a ɔbaa Jeremia hɔ wɔ Juda man nyina ho wɔ Josia ba Jehoiakim n'afe a otsia anan no mu; ɔnoara nye Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar n'afe a odzi kan no;, #2 Ahe 24.1; 2 Mbe 36.5-7; Dan 1.1
    2. ɔno na nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia kasaa kyerɛɛ Juda man no nyina na Jerusalɛm atsefo nyinara, dɛ, JER.25.3, Ofi Ammon ba Josia, Judahen no, n'afe a otsia duebiasa no mu, dze bodu ndɛ, mfe eduonu ebiasa nye yi, na EWURADZE n'asɛm aba mo do, na makasa makyerɛ hom, morosoɛr ahema na merekasa; na mbom hom enntsie.
    3. Na EWURADZE asoma no nkowaa nkɔnhyɛfo no nyina wɔ hom nkyɛn, ɔsoɛr ahema na ɔsoma hɔn, na hom enntsie, eso hom ammbrɛ hom aso adze, JER.25.5, wɔreka dɛ, Hom nsensan mfifi hom mu obiara no kwan bɔn do, na hom ndzeyɛɛ bɔn no mu, na hom ntsena asaase a EWURADZE dze ama hom na hom egyanom, ofir tsetse kesi daapem no do mpo:
    4. na mma hom nnkedzi abosom afofor ekyir nnkɔsom hɔn, na wɔnnsɔr hɔn, na hom mmfa hom nsaano edwuma nnyi me ebufuw; na mennkɛyɛ hom bɔn bi.
    5. Naaso hom enntsie me, EWURADZE na ɔse; ama hom dze hom nsaano edwuma eeyi me ebufuw ayɛ homara homho bɔn.
    6. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE se nye yi: Osiandɛ hom enntsie me nsɛm ntsi, JER.25.9, hwɛ, mobɔsoma ma wɔakɛfa kwaamu afamu mbusua nyina, EWURADZE na ɔse, na masoma hɔn akɛma Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar, m'akowaa no, na medze hɔn maba asaase yi, na no mu atsefo nyina do, na amanaman a wɔabɔ ho aprɔw nyina do, na masɛɛ hɔn huntuhuntu, na mama wɔadan ahobowdze, na asesardze, na daa amamfo.
    7. Bio so mibeyi ehurusi ndze na enyigye ndze, ayeforkun ndze, na ayefor ndze, ewuyambo nka, na kandzea ne kan mefi hɔn mu., #Jer 7.34; 16.9; Nyi 18.22
    8. Na asaase yi nyina bɛyɛ amamfo na ahobowdze; na amanaman yi bɔsom Babilɔnhen mfe eduosuon.
    9. Na ɔbɛba dɛ sɛ mfe eduosuon no wie so a, mebɛtsea Babilɔnhen na ɔman no, EWURADZE na ɔse, wɔ hɔn emumuyɛ ntsi, na Kaldeafo asaase no; na mebɛyɛ no amamfo afebɔɔ.
    10. Na mebɛma me nsɛm a maka etsia asaase no nyina aba mu, mekyerɛ dza wɔakyerɛw no buukuu yi mu no nyina a Jeremia ahyɛ ho nkɔm etsia amanaman nyina no.
    11. Na amanaman pii na ahemfo akɛse dze hɔn bɔsom hɔnho, mekyerɛ hɔnara a: na mebɛhyɛ hɔn dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ndzeyɛɛ na hɔn nsaano edwuma tse.
    12. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn se me nye yi: Gye ebufuw yi ne nsa kɔɔpow no wɔ me nsamu, na ma amanaman nyina a morosoma wo hɔn nkyɛn no wɔnnom.
    13. Na wɔbɔnom, na wɔato ntentan, na woegyingyim, osian afona a mobɔsoma no aba hɔn mu no ntsi.
    14. Nna megyee kɔɔpow no wɔ EWURADZE nsamu, na memaa amanaman a EWURADZE somaa me hɔn nkyɛn no nyina nomee:
    15. mekyerɛ, Jerusalɛm, na Juda nkurow, na n'ahemfo, na ne mbapɔmba, na wɔaayɛ amamfo ahobowdze, asesardze, na ndom, dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse, ndɛ yi.
    16. Egypthen Farao, na no nkowaa, na ne mbapɔmba, na ne man nyinara;
    17. na amamforafo nyinara na Uz asaase do ahemfo nyina, na Filistiafo asaase do ahemfo nyina; na Ashkelon, na Gaza, na Ekron, na Ashdod nkaa no;
    18. Edom, na Moab, na Ammonmba no;
    19. na Taere ahemfo nyina, na Zidon ahemfo nyina, na nsupruw a ɔwɔ po no egya no do ahemfo;
    20. Dedan, na Tema na Buz, na hɔn a woetwitwa ntakuwa nyina;
    21. na Arabia ahemfo nyina, na aforaforafo a wɔtse sar do no hɔn ahemfo nyina;
    22. na Zimri ahemfo nyina na Elam ahemfo nyina, na Media ahemfo nyina;
    23. na kwaamu afamu ahemfo nyina, hɔn a wɔbɛn na hɔn a wɔwɔ ekyirekyir, wɔnye hɔnho nkorkor, na wiadze nhenman horow a wɔwɔ asaase enyi nyina; na Sesakhen bedzi hɔn ekyir anom.
    24. Na ka kyerɛ hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn no se nye yi: Hom nnom, na hom mbobow, na hom mpuw ngu, na hom nhwehwe ase, na mma hom nnsoɛr bio, wɔ afona a morosoma aba hom mu no ntsi.
    25. Na sɛ ɔba dɛ wɔpow dɛ wɔgye kɔɔpow no wɔ wo nsamu nom a, ɔnodze ka kyerɛ hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE se nye yi: Ɔnom ara na hom bɔnom.
    26. Na, hwɛ, kurow a wɔdze me dzin ato no na mefitsi ase morobɔ no mbusu yi, na aso hom dze hom bɛfa hom ho edzi koraa? Hom remmfa hom ho nndzi: osiandɛ mebɛfrɛ afona maba asaase do atsefo nyina do: dɔm EWURADZE na ɔse.
    27. Dɛm ntsi hyɛ nsɛm yinom nyina ho nkɔm tsia hɔn, na se hɔn dɛ, EWURADZE befi sor bɔpɔw, na oefi no krɔnkrɔn tsenabea no do abɔ ne ndze mu; ɔbɔpɔw ɔdzendo wɔ no nguamban do; ɔbɛtseatsea mu dɛ wenyinaba wɔwfo wɔ asaase do mba nyina do.
    28. Dede bi bokodu asaase ano noho mpo; na EWURADZE nye amanaman enya ɔham, ɔnye adasa nyina enya atsɛn; na emumuyɛfo dze, obeyi hɔn ama afona, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    29. Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE se nye yi, Hwɛ mbusu retserɛw ba obefi ɔman do akɔ ɔman do, na ehum kɛse etu efi asaase etsiwa mu noho.
    30. Na da no EWURADZE n'atɔfoe bɛdeda hɔ fi asaase ne tsir ekesi asaase ne tsir kor do: worinngyam hɔn, eso wɔrommboaboa hɔn ano, eso worinnsie hɔn; wɔbɛyɛ dɛ efikyir egugu asaase enyi.
    31. Nguanhwɛfo e, hom mbɔ mbubuw na hom nkekamu ɛ; na hom nguankuw mu etsitsir, hom nyankanyankam nso mu: na hom okum nda no enya edu; na mobɔbobɔ hom posoposo, na hom abobɔ famu dɛ kuraba a ɔyɛ fɛw.
    32. Na nguanhwɛfo no nnkenya kwan eguan, eso nguankuw mu etsitsir no nnkefi nsa.
    33. Tsie nguanhwɛfo no hɔn su ne ndze bi, na nguankuw mu etsitsir mbubuwbɔ! Osiandɛ EWURADZE asɛɛ hɔn edzidzibea.
    34. Na suro ekitsa asomdwee nguamban no ɔnam EWURADZE n'ebufuhyew ntsi.
    35. Ɔadan ne dabew egya, dɛ ogyata: na hɔn asaase adan ahobowdze wɔ nhyɛdo afona no ne hyeehyew, na n'ebufuhyew ntsi.

    Tsir 26

    1. Josia ba Jehoiakim, Judahen no, n'ahendzi ahyɛse no, na asɛm yi fii EWURADZE nkyɛn bae, dɛ
    2. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Kegyina EWURADZE fie abanguado, na Juda nkurow nyinara a wɔba bɔsɔr EWURADZE fie no, ka nsɛm a mehyɛ wo dɛ ka kyerɛ hɔn no nyinara kyerɛ hɔn; mma mmfa asɛm biara nnsuma ekyir.
    3. Annyɛ a wobetsie, na hɔn mu nyimpa biara adan efi n'akwan bɔn no mu; ma meenu moho wɔ mbusu a mesua me tsirmu dɛ medze mobɔbɔ hɔn wɔ hɔn ndzeyɛɛ bɔn ntsi no ho.
    4. Na ka kyerɛ hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Sɛ hom enntsie me, dɛ hom bedzi me mbra a medze esi m'enyim no do, JER.26.5, dɛ hom betsie mo nkowaa nkɔnhyɛfo a mosoma hɔn hom nkyɛn a, mosoɛr ahema mpo na mosoma hɔn, na hom enntsie me nsɛm a;
    5. ɔnodze mebɛyɛ ofi yi dɛ Siloh, na mayɛ kurow yi ndom ama asaase do amanaman nyina.
    6. Na asɔfo na nkɔnhyɛfo na ɔman no nyina tsee dɛ Jeremia reka nsɛm yi wɔ EWURADZE fie.
    7. Na ɔbaa dɛ Jeremia wiee dza EWURADZE hyɛɛ no dɛ ɔnka nkyerɛ ɔman na asɔfo no, na nkɔnhyɛfo no, na ɔman no nyina suoo no mu, dɛ, Owu ara na obowu.
    8. Ebɛn ntsi na edze EWURADZE dzin ahyɛ nkɔm, dɛ, Ofi yi bɛyɛ dɛ Siloh na kurow yi ayɛ ekurofo a obi nntsena do? Na ɔman no nyinara behyiaa Jeremia nkyɛn wɔ EWURADZE fie.
    9. Na Juda mbapɔmba tsee ndzɛmba yinom no, wofii ahemfie fowee baa EWURADZE fie ɔponkɛse fofor no ano.
    10. Nna asɔfo no na nkɔnhyɛfo no kasaa kyerɛɛ mbapɔmba na ɔman no nyina, dɛ, Ɔbarimba yi sɛ owu; osiandɛ ɔahyɛ nkɔm etsia kurow yi, dɛ mbrɛ hom aso atse yi.
    11. Nna Jeremia kasaa kyerɛɛ mbapɔmba nyinara na ɔman no nyinara, dɛ, EWURADZE na ɔsomaa me dɛ membɛhyɛ asɛm a hom atse yi nyina ho nkɔm ntsia ofi yi na kurow yi.
    12. Dɛm ntsi afei hom nyeyɛ hom akwan na hom nyɛe yie, na hom ntsie EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ne ndze; na EWURADZE bonu noho wɔ mbusu a ɔaka etsia hom no ho.
    13. Na emi dze, hwɛ, mowɔ hom nsamu; hom nyɛ me dɛ mbrɛ oye na ɔtsen wɔ hom enyi do.
    14. Ohu ara na hom nhu no ampa dɛ, sɛ hom ku me a, hom dze bɔgya a odzi bem bɛba homankasa, na kurow yi, na no mu atsefo nyina do: na nokwar mu ara, EWURADZE na ɔasoma me hom nkyɛn dɛ membɛka nsɛm yi nyina wɔ hom asomu.
    15. Nna mbapɔmba na ɔman no nyina kaa kyerɛɛ asɔfo na nkɔnhyɛfo no dɛ: Ɔbarimba yi nnsɛ wu; osiandɛ EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn dzin mu na ɔakasa akyerɛ hɛn.
    16. Na binom fi asaase no do mpanyimfo no mu soɛree na wɔkaa kyerɛɛ ɔman baguafo no, dɛ, JER.26.18, Moresɛtnyi Mikaia hyɛɛ nkɔm wɔ Judahen Hezekia ne nda mu; na ɔkaa kyerɛɛ Judaman no nyina dɛ, Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE se nye yi: Wobofuntum Zion dɛ mfuwa, na Jerusalɛm adan ekurofo na ofi no ne bepɔw no ayɛ dɛ kwaa mu nsorɔnsorɔmbea.
    17. Aso Judahen Hezekia na Judafo nyina kum no? Ana nnyɛ EWURADZE na osuroo no, na ɔdze nkotoserɛ bisaa EWURADZE n'enyimpa, na EWURADZE so nuu noho wɔ mbusu a ɔkae tsiaa hɔn no ho. Dɛm na yɛdze bɔbɔ mbusu kɛse etsia hɛnankasa hɛn akra.
    18. Na ɔbarimba bi so wɔ hɔ a ɔhyɛɛ nkɔm wɔ EWURADZE dzin mu, Semaia a ofi Kiriat-jearim no ne ba Uria; na ɔhyɛɛ nkɔm tsiaa kurow yi na asaase yi, dɛ mbrɛ Jeremia ne nsɛm nyina tse:
    19. na ɔhen Jehoiakim, na ne mbarimba akatakyi nyinara, na mbapɔmba nyinara, wɔtsee ne nsɛm no, ɔhen no hwehwɛɛ dɛ oku no; na Uria tsee no, osuroi, na oguanee, na ɔkɔr Egypt:
    20. na ɔhen Jehoiakim somaa mbarimba bi kɔr Egypt, mekyerɛ Akbor ne ba Elnatan, na mbarimba bi wɔka no ho kɔr Egypt:
    21. na wɔkɛfaa Uria fii Egypt, na wɔdze no brɛɛ ɔhen Jehoiakim; ɔno na ɔdze afona kum no, na ɔtoow no fun kyeen amansuon esiei.
    22. Na Safan ba Ahikam ne nsa wɔ Jeremia afa, dɛ mma wonnyi no nnhyɛ ɔman no nsa mma wonnku no.

    Tsir 27

    1. Josia ba Jehoiakim, Judahen no, n'ahendzi ahyɛse no, na asɛm yi fi EWURADZE nkyɛn baa Jeremia hɔ, dɛ
    2. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Yɛ nkyehoma na adaban ma woho, na fa hyɛ wo kɔn;
    3. na fa mona Edomhen, na Moabhen, na Ammonmba hɔn hen, na Taerehen, na Sidonhen, wɔ abɔfo a wɔba Judahen Zedekia hɔ wɔ Jerusalɛm ne nsamu:
    4. na hyɛ hɔn ma wɔnkɛka nkyerɛ hɔn wuranom, dɛ, Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn no, se nye yi: Mbrɛ hom nkɛka nkyerɛ hom wuranom nye yi:
    5. Emi na medze m'ahoɔdzen kɛse na me basa a atsen mayɛ asaase, nyimpa na mbowa a wɔwɔ asaase enyi nyina; na medze ma obiara dɛ mbrɛ ɔtsen wɔ m'enyi do.
    6. Na afei medze asaase yi nyina mahyɛ m'akowaa Nebukadenezar, Babilɔnhen no, ne nsa; na wiramu mbowa so medze ama no dɛ wɔnsom no.
    7. Na amanaman nyina bɔsom ɔno na ne ba, na ne ba ne ba, ma ekodu dɛ noara so n'asaaseber bɔso: nna nkyii amanaman pii na ahemfo akɛse dze no bɔsom hɔnho.
    8. Na ɔbɛba dɛ, ɔman na ahendzi a wɔronnsom ɔno Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar, na wɔremmfa hɔn kɔn nnhyɛ Babilɔnhen no kɔndua ase no, medze afona na ɔkɔm na ɔyardɔm mebɛtsea ɔman no, ma ekodu dɛ menam ne nsa do mama wɔasa.
    9. Na hom dze, mma hom nntsie hom nkɔnhyɛfo, na hom mbusu nkɔnhyɛfo, na hom abayifo a wɔkasa kyerɛ hom, dɛ, Hom ronnsom Babilɔnhen no:
    10. na nkɔntor na wɔhyɛ hom, ama woeeyi hom efi hom asaase do akɔ ekyirekyir, na maapam hom na hom aahera.
    11. Na ɔman a wɔdze hɔn kɔn bɛhyɛ Babilɔnhen kɔndua ase, na wɔasom no no, ɔman no na mebɛma wɔaka hɔnankasa asaase do, EWURADZE na ɔse; na wɔadɔw do, na wɔatsena do.
    12. Na mekasaa kyerɛɛ Judahen Zedekia dɛ, Mbrɛ nsɛm yi nyina tse, dɛ, Hom mfa hom kɔn nhyɛ Babilɔnhen no kɔndua no ase, na hom nsom ɔno na ne man, na hom atsena ase.
    13. Ebɛn ntsi na hom bowu, ɔwo na wo man, wɔ afona, ɔkɔm na ɔyardɔm ano, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE aka wɔ ɔman a wɔronnsom Babilɔnhen ho no?
    14. Na mma hom nntsie nsɛm a nkɔnhyɛfo no ka kyerɛ hom, dɛ, Hom ronnsom Babilɔnhen no: na nkɔntor na wɔhyɛ hom.
    15. Na nnyɛ emi na masoma hɔn, EWURADZE na ɔse, na wɔdze me dzin hyɛ ator nkɔm; ama maapam hom, na hom aahera, hom na nkɔnhyɛfo a wɔhyɛ hom nkɔm no nyina.
    16. Eso mekaa mekyerɛɛ asɔfo no, na ɔman yi nyina, dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Mma hom nntsie nsɛm a hom nkɔnhyɛfo a wɔhyɛ hom nkɔm no ka dɛ, Hwɛ, ɔrennkyɛr na wɔdze EWURADZE fie nkɔɔpow no efi Babilɔn asan aba no: na nkɔntor na wɔhyɛ hom.
    17. Mma hom nntsie hɔn; hom nsom Babilɔnhen, na hom ntsena ase: ebɛn ntsi na kurow yi ndan amamfo?
    18. Na sɛ wɔyɛ nkɔnhyɛfo, na EWURADZE asɛm wɔ hɔn nkyɛn a, ma wɔnkotow nserɛ dɔm EWURADZE, dɛ mma nkɔɔpow no a aka EWURADZE fie, na Judahen ne fie, na Jerusalɛm no, aannkɔ Babilɔn.
    19. Na mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE se wɔ edum no na po no na afɔrmbukyia no na nkɔɔpow nkaa a woegya no kurow yi mu ho nye yi, JER.27.20, dza Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar ammfa annkɔ ber a ɔsoaa Jehoiakim ba Jekonia, Judahen no, na Juda na Jerusalɛm mbapɔmba kɔr Babilɔn no;
    20. nyew, mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn se wɔ nkɔɔpow a aka EWURADZE fie, na Judahen fie, na Jerusalɛm ho nye yi;
    21. Wɔbɔsoa akɔ Babilɔn, na hɔ na ɔbɛtsena ekodu da a mebɛkɛsera no, EWURADZE na ɔse, ɔno na medze no bɛsan aba bea yi do bio.

    Tsir 28

    1. Na ɔbaa afe no ara mu, Judahen Zedekia n'ahendzi ahyɛse, afe a otsia anan no, bosoom a otsia enum no mu, dɛ nkɔnhyɛnyi Azzur ba Hanania a ofi Gibeon no, ɔsee me wɔ EWURADZE fie, wɔ asɔfo no na ɔman no nyina enyim, dɛ
    2. Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn ka nye dɛ, Mebubu Babilɔnhen no kɔndua no.
    3. Mfe ebien mu ara pɛr na medze EWURADZE fie nkɔɔpow a Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar bɛfae fii bea yi do kɔr Babilɔn no nyinara bɛsan aba bea yi do bio:
    4. na medze Jehoiakim ba, Jekonia, Judahen no, na Juda ndɔmmumfo a wɔkɔr Babilɔn no nyina mebɛsan aba bea yi do bio, EWURADZE na ɔse: na mubobubu Babilɔnhen no kɔndua no.
    5. Nna nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia see nkɔnhyɛnyi Hanania wɔ asɔfo no enyim, na ɔman a wogyinagyina EWURADZE fie no nyina enyim, JER.28.6, mekyerɛ nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia see dɛ, Amen: EWURADZE nyɛ sa: EWURADZE mma wo nsɛm a ahyɛ nkɔm aka dɛ wɔdze EWURADZE fie nkɔɔpow, na ndɔmmumfo no nyina befi Babilɔn asan aba bea yi do mbra mu.
    6. Naaso afei tsie asɛm yi a mereka wɔ w'asomu, na ɔman yi nyina asomu yi:
    7. nkɔnhyɛfo a wodzi m'enyim na w'enyim fi tsetse no, wɔhyehyɛɛ asaase pii, na ahendzi akɛse, akodzi, na mbusu, na ɔyardɔm ho nkɔm.
    8. Nkɔnhyɛnyi a ɔhyɛ asomdwee ho nkɔm no, sɛ nkɔnhyɛnyi no n'asɛm no ba mu a, nna wɔdze hu nkɔnhyɛnyi a EWURADZE asoma no nokwar mu.
    9. Nna nkɔnhyɛnyi Hanania yii ɔdaban no fii nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia no kɔn mu, na obubuu mu.
    10. Na Hanania kae wɔ ɔman no nyina enyim, dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Dɛmara na mubobubu Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar no kɔndua no mefi amanaman nyina hɔn mu mfe ebien ara pɛr mu. Na nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia kɔr no kwan.
    11. Na nkɔnhyɛnyi Hanania bubuu ɔdaban no fii nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia kɔn mu no ekyir no, nna EWURADZE asɛm baa Jeremia nkyɛn, dɛ, JER.28.13, Kɔ, kɛse Hanania, dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Ebubu dua adaban no; na ebɛyɛ dadze adaban ahyɛ ananmu.
    12. Na mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn no, se nye yi: Medze dadze kɔndua mato amanaman yi nyina kɔn mu, dɛ wɔnsom Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar: na wɔbɔsom no: na medze wiramu mbowa so mama no.
    13. Nna nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia see nkɔnhyɛnyi Hanania dɛ, Hanania, afei tsie; EWURADZE annsoma wo; na ɔwo ema ɔman yi dze hɔnho twer atorsɛm.
    14. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Hwɛ, mubotu wo efi asaase enyi: afe yi ibowu, osiandɛ aka etuatsewsɛm etsia EWURADZE.
    15. Dɛmara na nkɔnhyɛnyi Hanania wuu afe no ara mu bosoom a otsia esuon no mu.

    Tsir 29

    1. Na iyinom nye nsɛm a ɔwɔ nwoma a nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia fi Jerusalɛm dze monaa ndɔmmumfo no mu mpanyimfo no nkaa no, na asɔfo no, na nkɔnhyɛfo no, na nkorɔfo nyinara a Nebukadenezar soaa hɔn fii Jerusalɛm kɔr Babilɔn ndɔmmum no:
    2. (ber a ɔhen Jekonia, na ɔhen ne na, na epiafo no, na Juda na Jerusalɛm mbapɔmba no, na edwimfo no, na atomfo no fii Jerusalɛm kɔree no:)
    3. ɔdze nam Safan ba Elasa na Hilkia ba Gemaria (a Judahen Zedekia somaa no kɔr Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar hɔ wɔ Babilɔn no, ) ne nsa do, dɛ, JER.29.4, Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn se ndɔmmumfo nyina a mama wɔasoa hɔn akɔ Babilɔn ndɔmmum no nye yi:
    4. hom nsisi adan ntsenatsena mu; na hom ntsetsɛw nture, na hom ndzi hɔn mu aba;
    5. hom nwarwar, na hom nwowo mbabanyin na mbabaa; na hom ngyegye yernom mma hom mbabanyin, na hom mfa hom mbabaa mma kunnom na wɔnwowo mbabanyin na mbabaa; na hom ndɔr wɔ hɔ, na hom ho eennsuar.
    6. Na hom nhwehwɛ kurow a mama wɔasoa hom akɔ hɔ ndɔmmum no n'amandwee, na hom nyi EWURADZE mpaa mma no: na n'amandwee mu na hom benya asomdwee.
    7. Na mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn se nye yi: Mma hom mma nkɔnhyɛfo a wɔwɔ hom mu no, na adzehufo no ndaadaa hom, eso mma hom nntsie adaaso a hom ma wɔso no.
    8. Na ator mu na wɔdze me dzin hyɛ hom nkɔm: monnsoma hɔn, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    9. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Mfe eduosuon nya du ma Babilɔn a mebɛserɛ hom, na mama m'asɛmpa aba mu ama hom, dɛ mebɛma hom asan aba ha bio.
    10. Na minyim adwen a modwen wɔ hom ho, EWURADZE na ɔse, asomdwee adwen a, na nnyɛ mbusu adwen bi a, dɛ mebɛma hom enyidado wɔ hom ewiei.
    11. Na hom bɛfrɛ me, na hom akɔ na hom eyi mpaa ama me, na metsie hom.
    12. Na hom bɔhwehwɛ me, na hom ehu me, ber a hom dze hom akoma nyina bɔhwehwɛ m'ekyir kwan no.
    13. Na mebɛma hom ehu me, EWURADZE na ɔse, na medze hom ndɔmmum masan maba, na maboa hom ano efi amanaman nyina mu, na mbea nyina a mapam hom makɔ hɔ no mu, EWURADZE na ɔse; na medze hom aba mbea a memaa wɔsoaa hom fir kɔr ndɔmmum no bio.
    14. Na hom aka dɛ, EWURADZE ama nkɔnhyɛfo no do ama hɛn wɔ Babilɔn.
    15. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE ka wɔ ɔhen a ɔtse David akɔngua do, na ɔman no nyina a wɔtse kurow yi mu, hom nuanom a wɔnnye hom ronnkɔ ndɔmmum ho nye yi;
    16. mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE se nye yi: Hwɛ, mebɛma afona, ɔkɔm, na ɔyardɔm aba hɔn do, na mayɛ hɔn dɛ adɔmba prɔwee a, muo a omuo dodow ntsi, wodzi a ɔnnyɛ.
    17. Na medze afona, ɔkɔm, na ɔyardɔm betsiw hɔn, na meyi hɔn ama ma wɔatow hɔn edzi akɔnaaba wɔ asaase do nhenman nyina mu, na mayɛ ekyiwadze na ahobowdze, na asesardze, na ahorohoraadze wɔ amanaman nyina a mapam hɔn makɔ hɔ nyina mu:
    18. osiandɛ woenntsie me nsɛm a, EWURADZE na ɔse, medze mosomaa mo nkowaa nkɔnhyɛfo no baa hɔn nkyɛn, mosoɛɛr ahema na mosomaa hɔn; na hom enntsie, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    19. Dɛm ntsi hom ndɔmmumfo a mama hom efi Jerusalɛm akɔ Babilɔn nyinara, hom ntsie EWURADZE n'asɛm.
    20. Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn se wɔ Kolaia ba Ahab, na Maaseia ba Zedekia a wɔdze me dzin hyɛɛ nkɔntor ho nye yi: Hwɛ, mibeyi hɔn ahyɛ Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar nsa; na woeku hɔn wɔ hom enyim;
    21. na hɔn na wɔdze hɔn bɛyɛ ndom wɔ Juda ndɔmmumfo a wɔwɔ Babilɔn nyina anomu, dɛ, EWURADZE nyɛ wo dɛ Zedekia na Ahab a Babilɔnhen hoow hɔn wɔ ogya mu no:
    22. osiandɛ woedzi nkwaseasɛm wɔ Israel, na wɔafefa hɔn nsɛfo yernom, na wɔdze me dzin aka atorsɛm a nnyɛ emi na mehyɛɛ hɔn; na emi na minyim, na emi nye ɔdasefo, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    23. Na ka wɔ Nehelamnyi Semaia ho, dɛ, JER.29.25, Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn se nye yi; dɛ, Osiandɛ amona nwoma wɔ wankasa wo dzin mu akɛma ɔman a wɔwɔ Jerusalɛm nyina, na ɔsɔfo Zefania Maaseia ba no, na asɔfo no nyinara, dɛ, JER.29.26, EWURADZE ahyɛ wo ɔsɔfo wɔ ɔsɔfo Jehoiada ananmu, dɛ hom nyɛ asomfo wɔ EWURADZE fie mma nyimpa biara a ɔabɔ dam, na ɔyɛ noho nkɔnhyɛnyi, na edze no ato dua mu na mpokyerɛ mu.
    24. Na afei, ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na enntwuw Anathotnyi Jeremia a ɔyɛ noho hom nkɔnhyɛnyi no n'enyim, JER.29.28, susuampa dɛ ɔasoma aba hɛn nkyɛn wɔ Babilɔn dɛ, Ndɔmmum no akyɛr: hom nsisi adan, na hom ntsena mu; na hom ntsetsɛw nture, na hom ndzi mu aba?
    25. Na ɔsɔfo Zefania kenkaan nwoma yi wɔ nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia asomu.
    26. Nna EWURADZE n'asɛm baa Jeremia hɔ, dɛ, JER.29.31, Soma ma wɔnkɔ ndɔmmumfo no nyina hɔ, dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se wɔ Nehelamnyi Semaia ho nye yi: Osiandɛ Semaia ahyɛ hom nkɔm, na mannsoma no, na ɔama hom atwer atorsɛm ntsi;
    27. dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Hwɛ, mebɛtsea Nehelamnyi Semaia na n'asefo; orinnya barimba biara ma ɔnntsena ɔman yi mu, eso orunnhu yie a medze mebɛyɛ ɔman yi, EWURADZE na ɔse: osiandɛ ɔaka etuatsewsɛm etsia EWURADZE.

    Tsir 30

    1. Asɛm a ofi EWURADZE nkyɛn baa Jeremia hɔ, dɛ, JER.30.2, Mbrɛ EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn se nye yi, dɛ, Kyerɛw nsɛm a maka makyerɛ wo nyina wɔ nwoma mu.
    2. Na, hwɛ, nda reba a, EWURADZE na ɔse, medze me man Israel na Juda ndɔmmumfo bɛsan aba, EWURADZE na ɔse: na mama wɔasan asaase a medze memaa hɔn egyanom no do, na woenya edzi.
    3. Na yinom nye nsɛm a EWURADZE kae wɔ Israel ho na Juda ho.
    4. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Yɛatse ahopopo ndze, na suro nka, na nnyɛ asomdwee dze bi a.
    5. Afei hom mbisa na hom nhu kyerɛ dɛ ɔbarimba botum awo ba anaa: ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na muhu ɔbarimba biara dɛ ne nsa dze ne sisiw mu dɛ ɔbaa a awoo aka no yi? Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na enyim nyinara atotow fitaa yi?
    6. Due! Na da no yɛ hu dodow a biara nntse dɛ ɔno: Jakob no fona ber a; naaso wɔbɛgye no nkwa efi mu.
    7. Na ɔbɛba dɛ da no mu no, Dɔm EWURADZE na ɔse, mubobubu no kɔndua efi wo kɔn ho, na matsetsew wo nkyehoma no mu; na ananaben nnkedzi no nya bio:
    8. na wɔbɔsom EWURADZE hɔn Nyankopɔn, na hɔn hen David a mebɛma no do ama hɔn no.
    9. Dɛm ntsi m'akowaa Jakob, mma nnsuro, EWURADZE na ɔse; eso, Israel, mma wo bo nntu: na, hwɛ, mebɛgye wo nkwa mefi ekyirekyir na w'asefo mefi hɔn ndɔmmumfafo asaase do; na Jakob bɛsan aba, ebenya asomdwee na ahotɔ, na obiara rinnyi no hu., #Jer 46.27
    10. Na menye wo nam, EWURADZE na ɔse, dɛ mebɛgye wo nkwa: na mebɛma amanaman a mabɔ wo apetse hɔ nyina asa koraa, na ɔwoara dze, meremma ennsa koraa; na mbom medze atsɛmbu mebɛtsea wo, na meremma emmfa woho tɔtrɔtɔ ara da.
    11. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Wo pira nnyi edur, na wo pirakur adzen wo.
    12. Obi nnyi hɔ a odzi w'asɛm ma wo ayarsadur biara innyi hɔ ma w'epirakur, na ayarsa biara innyi hɔ ma wo.
    13. W'adɔfo nyinara werɛ efir wo; wɔnnhwehwɛ wo: osiandɛ medze ɔtamfo epirakur mepira wo, medze otsiɔdzennyi ntsea matsea wo; wɔ w'emumuyɛ ne kɛse ntsi, osiandɛ wo bɔn adɔɔ so pii.
    14. Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na erekeka mu wɔ wo pira ntsi? Wo kur nnyi edur: wɔ w'emumuyɛ ne kɛse ntsi, osiandɛ wo bɔn adɔɔ so ntsi na medze ndzɛmba yinom ayɛ wo.
    15. Dɛm ntsi hɔn a wɔmemen wo nyina wɔbɛmen hɔn; na w'atamfo no nyinara mu obiara bɔkɔ ndɔmmum; na hɔn a wɔsoɛr wo no wɔbɔsoɛr hɔn do; na hɔn a wɔfa wo afo nyinara wɔbɛfa hɔn afo.
    16. Na mebɛma wo apɔwmudzen bio, na masa w'epirakur, EWURADZE na ɔse; osiandɛ wɔafrɛ wo nyia woeyi no tokyen, dɛ, Zion a obi nnhwehwɛ n'ekyir kwan a.
    17. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Hwɛ, medze Jakob ntamadan mu ndɔmmum mebɛsan aba bio, na menya ayamuhyehye wɔ ne tsenabea ho; na wɔbɛkyekyer kurow no wɔ ne ndamfo no ara do, na ahemfi no besi hɔ dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse no ara.
    18. Na ndaase na hɔn a hɔn enyi agye ndze befir edzi wɔ mu: na mebɛma wɔadɔr, na worunnsuar; mebɛhyɛ hɔn enyimnyam so, na wonnkobu hɔn enyimtsia.
    19. Hɔn mba so bɛyɛ dɛ asɔpɔn no, na hɔn mboanofo betsim wɔ m'enyim, na mebɛtsea hɔn a wɔhaw hɔn no nyinara.
    20. Na hɔn hen bɛyɛ hɔnankasa hɔn bi, na hɔn hwɛdofo efir hɔn mu; na mebɛma wɔatwe epin me, na wɔbɛbɛn me nkyɛn: na woana nye nyia woesi no bo dɛ ɔbɛbɛn me? EWURADZE na ɔse.
    21. Na hom bɛyɛ me man, na emi mayɛ hom Nyankopɔn.
    22. Hwɛ, EWURADZE n'ehum, mekyerɛ n'ebufuhyew no, etu, ekyinehyia ehum a: obotu abɔ emumuyɛfo etsifi.
    23. EWURADZE n'ebufuw hyeehyew no rennsan, gyedɛ oewie yɛ, na ɔama n'akoma mu esusudze aba mu ansaana. Nda a odzi ekyir no mu na hom bɛtse ase.

    Tsir 31

    1. Aber no mu no, EWURADZE na ɔse, mebɛyɛ Israel mbusuakuw no nyina hɔn Nyankopɔn, na hɔn so wɔayɛ me man.
    2. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Ɔman a afona daan hɔn gyae no, enya adom wɔ sar no do; mekyerɛ Israel, ber a memaa onyaa ahomgye no a.
    3. EWURADZE yii noho kyerɛɛ me tsetse, dɛ, Ampaara, madɔ wo ɔdomankoma dɔ: dɛm ntsi na medze adɔyɛ atwe wo no.
    4. Mibesi wo bio, na esi hɔ, Ao Israel ɔbaabun: edze wo mpintsin bɛgyegye w'enyi bio, na epue wɔ agofo asaw mu.
    5. Ebɛtsetsɛw wenyin nture wɔ Samaria mbepɔw do bio: atsetsɛwfo bɛtsetsɛw, na woedzi n'aba bi.
    6. Na da bi bɛba a aweɔmfo bɛtsea mu wɔ Efraim mbepɔw do, dɛ, Hom nsoɛr ma yɛmfow nkɔ EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn nkyɛn wɔ Zion.
    7. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Hom mfa enyigye ntow ndwom wɔ Jakob ho, na hom mbɔ amanaman etsitsir ho ose: hom mfa ntahye, hom nyi ayɛw, na hom nse dɛ, EWURADZE, gye wo man, Israel nkaa no nkwa.
    8. Hwɛ, medze hɔn fi kwaamu afamu asaase do mebɛba, na makɔboa hɔn ano efi asaase ano noho, na enyifurafo na mpakye, ɔpemfo na ɔbaa a ɔroko awoo nyina ka ho bi: okuw kukuankoma na wɔbɛsan aba ha.
    9. Wɔdze osu bɛba, na nkotoserɛ na medze bɛgye hom nkwa: mebɛma wɔanantsew esutsen ho, wɔ ɔkwan tsenee mu a worimmfintsiw: na meyɛ egya ma Israel, na Efraim nye m'abakan.
    10. Amanaman, hom ntsie EWURADZE n'asɛm, na hom nka wɔ esupruw a ɔwɔ ekyirekyir no mu; dɛ, Nyia ɔbɔɔ Israel petsee no, ɔbɔboaboa n'ano, na wɔahwɛ no do, dɛ mbrɛ oguanhwɛfo hwɛ no nguankuw do no.
    11. Na EWURADZE agye Jakob, na ɔapon no efi nyia ɔkyɛn no ahoɔdzen no nsamu.
    12. Na wɔbɛba abɔtow ndwom wɔ Zion sorɔnsorɔmbea, na wɔapem akɔ EWURADZE ne yieyɛ ho, eburow, na nsa, na ngo, na hɔn nguan na anantwimba ho: na hɔn kra bɛyɛ dɛ ture a woegugu mu nsu; na worinndzi awerɛhow bio koraa.
    13. Nna nkataasia enyi bɛgye asaw mu, na mberantsɛ na nkɔdaa nyinara abɔ mu enyi agye: na mebɛdan hɔn nkɔmbɔdzi ahosɛpɛw, na makyekye hɔn werɛ na mama woefi hɔn awerɛhow mu edzi ehurusi.
    14. Na mebɛma angoanam amee asɔfo hɔn kra, na me yieyɛ amee me man, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    15. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Wɔtse ndze bi nka wɔ Rama, osukwadwom, na osu wenwen, Rakel rusu ne mba; na ɔmmpen dɛ wɔbɛkyekye no werɛ wɔ ne mba ntsi; osiandɛ wonnyi hɔ.
    16. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Sianka wo ndze wɔ osu ho, na w'enyiwa wɔ nyinsuwa ho: na w'edwuma ho akatua wɔ hɔ, EWURADZE na ɔse: na wobefi ɔtamfo no asaase do aba bio.
    17. Na enyidado wɔ hɔ ma w'ewiei, EWURADZE na ɔse; na wo mba bɛsan aba hɔnankasa hɔn aman do bio.
    18. Nyew, matse Efraim no nkɔmbɔdzi dɛ, Ɔwo atsea me na magye ntsea no, meyɛɛ dɛ ɔnantwiba a ɔnnweaa kɔndua ho. Fa me san bra, ma mensan mbra; na ɔwo nye EWURADZE me Nyankopɔn.
    19. Ampaara me nsankyir ekyir no, munuu moho; na wɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ me no, mutwaa m'aserɛ ho: m'enyi toe, nyew, m'enyim guu ase mpo, osiandɛ mosoaa me mberantsɛber mu enyimguase.
    20. Aso Efraim yɛ me dɔba? Aso ɔyɛ ɔba a m'enyi gye no ho? Mpɛn dodow ara a mekasa tsia no no, nkaa ara na meda ho mekaa no: dɛm ntsi mo nson mu burbur me wɔ no ho; mubohu no mbɔbɔr ampaara, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    21. Sisi ɔkwanmu nsewhyɛdze ma woho, sisi ɔkwankyerɛ edum ma woho: fa w'akoma si tsempɔn no no do, ɔkwan a efaa mu no a. San bra, Israel ɔbaabun, san bra wo nkurow yi mu bio.
    22. Ɔwo ekyirsannyi babaa, ibedzi akɔnaaba ekodu dabɛn ara? Na EWURADZE abɔ adze fofor wɔ asaase do, Ɔbaa botwitwa agye barimba.
    23. Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn no, se nye yi: Wɔbɛda ho aka asɛm yi bio wɔ Juda asaase do na no nkurow mu, ber a medze hɔn efi ndɔmmum asan aba no dɛ: Ao Pɛrpɛr tsenabea, krɔnkrɔnyɛ bepɔw, EWURADZE nhyira wo!
    24. Na Juda na no nkurow nyinara bɔbɔ mu atsena mu; ekuafo, na hɔn a wɔnye mbowakuw kyinkyin.
    25. Na mama ɔkra a ɔaberɛ amee, na ɔkra werɛhofo biara mahyɛ no ma bio.
    26. Iyi do na minyanee, na mohwɛe; na me nda tɔɔ me dɛw mu.
    27. Hwɛ, nda reba a, EWURADZE na ɔse, medze ɔdasanyi n'asefo, na abowa n'asefo mubodua Israel fi na Juda fi.
    28. Na ɔbɛba dɛ, dɛ mbrɛ m'enyi asa hɔn do dɛ mubotutu na mebubu, na mebutuw na masɛɛ, na mehiahia ho no; dɛmara so na m'enyi bɔko hɔn ho dɛ mibesi na matsɛw, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    29. Nda no mu no wɔnnkɛka bio dɛ, Egyanom atwɛr ebuntwirede yerɛyerɛw, na mba hɔn se afemfem.
    30. Na mbom obiara bowu wɔ nankasa n'emumuyɛ ntsi: nyimpa biara a obedzi ebuntwirede yerɛyerɛw no, ɔnoara ne se na ɔbɛfem.
    31. Hwɛ, nda reba a, EWURADZE na ɔse, menye Israel fi na Juda fi bedzi ahyɛmu fofor:
    32. ɔnntse dɛ ahyɛmu a menye hɔn egyanom dzii wɔ da a musuoo hɔn nsamu no, miyii hɔn Egypt asaase do no; m'ahyɛmu a wɔtoe, naaso na emi dze meda ho meyɛ hɔn kun no, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    33. Na iyi nye ahyɛmu a menye Israel fi bedzi wɔ nda no ekyir, EWURADZE na ɔse; medze me mbra bɛhyɛ hɔn mu, na hɔn akoma mu na mebɛkyerɛw mu; na emi mebɛyɛ hɔn Nyankopɔn, na hɔn so wɔayɛ me man:
    34. na obiara nnkɛkyerɛ ne nyɛnko, na obiara nnkɛkyerɛ no nua bio dɛ, Hu EWURADZE: na hɔn nyinara wobohu no, ofi hɔn mu aketseaba do kesi hɔn mu kɛse do, EWURADZE na ɔse: na medze hɔn emumuyɛ mebɛkyɛ hɔn, na hɔn bɔn so merennkaa bio.
    35. Mbrɛ EWURADZE a ɔma ewia hyerɛn adzekyee, na ɔhyehyɛ bosoom na nworaba ma wɔhyerɛn anadwe, onunu po mu ma n'asorɛkye hur, a ne dzin dze dɔm EWURADZE no, ɔse nye yi:
    36. Sɛ ahyehyɛdze yinom fi m'enyim fir a, EWURADZE na ɔse, ɔnodze na Israel asefo so begyaa dɛ wɔyɛ ɔman wɔ m'enyim daa nyina.
    37. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Sɛ wotum susu ɔsor wimu, na wɔbɔr hwehwɛ asaase ne fapem wɔ n'ase noho a, ɔnodze na mo so mobɔtow Israel asefo akyen wɔ dza wɔayɛ nyina ntsi, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    38. Hwɛ, nda reba a, EWURADZE na ɔse, wɔbɛkyekyer kurow no ama EWURADZE, efi Hananel abantsentsen ho ekodu nkyɛnmu ɔponkɛse no ho.
    39. Na susuhoma no befi hɔ ara nam tsentsendo ekodu Gareb koko ho, na oebu adan ekesi Goa.
    40. Na efun na nso bɔnsa no nyina, na mfuwa nyina a okodu ɔwora Kidron ho, dze kodu pɔnkɔ ɔponkɛse no nkyɛn no wɔ boka afamu, wɔbɛyɛ krɔnkrɔn ama EWURADZE; worunntutu, eso worunndwuruw nngu famu dabiarada.

    Tsir 32

    1. Asɛm a ofi EWURADZE nkyɛn baa Jeremia hɔ wɔ Judahen Zedekia n'afe a otsia du no a, ɔyɛ Nebukadenezar n'afe a otsia duawɔtwe no mu no.
    2. Aber no na nkyii Babilɔnhen no dɔm kotuaa Jerusalɛm: na wɔdze nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia too efiadze wɔ ɔweɔmfo bagua no a ɔwɔ Judahen ne fie no mu.
    3. Na Judahen Zedekia dze no too efiadze, dɛ, Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na ehyɛ nkɔm, na eka dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Hwɛ, medze kurow yi mebɛhyɛ Babilɔnhen nsa, ma ɔagye;
    4. na Judahen Zedekia rimmfi Kaldeafo nsa, na oyi ara na wobeyi no ahyɛ Babilɔnhen nsa, na ɔnye no akasa ano na ano, na n'enyi ehu n'enyi;
    5. na obegya Zedekia akɔ Babilɔn, na hɔ na ɔbɛtsena ekodu dɛ mebɛsera no, EWURADZE na ɔse: kaansa hom nye Kaldeafo ko mpo a, orunnwie hom yie.
    6. Na Jeremia see dɛ, EWURADZE n'asɛm baa mo hɔ, dɛ, JER.32.7, Hwɛ, wo wɔfa Sallum ne ba Hanamel bɛba wo nkyɛn, dɛ, Tɔ mo mfuwa a ɔwɔ Anathot no; na ɔwo na no pon ho kwan dzi wɔ wo dɛ ebɔtɔ.
    7. Nna mo wɔfa ba Hanamel baa me nkyɛn wɔ aweɔmfo abangua no do, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE n'asɛm tse no na ɔsee me dɛ, Meserɛ wo, tɔ mo mfuwa a ɔwɔ Anathot a ɔwɔ Benjamin asaase do no: na ɔwo na adze no ne dzi yɛ wodze, na no pon dzi wɔ wo; tɔ ma woho. Nna muhun dɛ EWURADZE asɛm no nye no.
    8. Na motɔɔ asaase a ɔwɔ Anathot no wɔ mo wɔfa ba Hanamel hɔ, na mikeer dwɛɛtɛɛ no memaa no, mekyerɛ dwetɛ dwetɛbona duesuon.
    9. Na mekyerɛɛw no wɔ nwoma mu, na mosɔɔw ano, na mefrɛɛ adasefo, na mikeer dwɛɛtɛɛ no wɔ nsɛn mu memaa no.
    10. Nna mefaa ɔtɔ nwoma no, dza wɔsɔɔw ano, dɛ mbrɛ mbra na atɔrmuadze se no, na dza n'ano da hɔ no nyina:
    11. na medze ɔtɔ nwoma no mehyɛɛ Maseia ba Neria ne ba Baruk nsa, wɔ no wɔfa ba Hanamel n'enyim, na adasefo a wɔdze hɔn nsa hyɛɛ ɔtɔ nwoma no ase wɔ Juda a wɔtsetse ɔweɔmfo abanguado hɔ nyina enyim no enyim.
    12. Na mehyɛɛ Baruk wɔ hɔn enyim, dɛ, JER.32.14, Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn se nye yi: Fa nwoma iyinom, ɔtɔ nwoma yi, dza wɔasɔw ano, na nwoma yi a n'ano da hɔ nyinara, na fa hyɛ dɛtsesɛn bi mu; na ɔaakyɛr nda pii.
    13. Na mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn, se nye yi: Wɔbɛda ho atotɔ adan, na mfuwa, na wenyin nture wɔ asaase yi do bio.
    14. Afei medze ɔtɔ nwoma no maa Neria ba Baruk n'ekyir no, miyii mpaa maa EWURADZE, dɛ, JER.32.17, Ao EWURADZE Nyankopɔn! Hwɛ, ɔwo na edze wo tum kɛse na wo basa a atsen yɛɛ ɔsor na asaase; biribiara nnyɛ wo yɛ na:
    15. ɔwo a ekyerɛ mbɔbɔrhu ma mpempem, na itua egyanom hɔn emumuyɛ kaw gu hɔn mba a wodzi hɔn ekyir hɔn bo mu: ne dzin dze ɔkɛse, Onyankopɔn katakyi, dɔm EWURADZE:
    16. apam mu ɔkɛse, ndwuma mu ɔkatakyi: ɔwo w'enyiwa bue wɔ adasamba akwan nyina do; dɛ edze bɛma obiara dɛ mbrɛ n'akwan tse, na dɛ mbrɛ ne ndzeyɛɛ aba tse:
    17. ɔwo emaa nsɛnkyerɛdze na anwanwadze sii Egypt asaase do, dze bodu ndɛ da yi mpo, wɔ Israel na amanaman nyina mu; na edze gyee dzin maa woho, dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse ndɛ da yi;
    18. na edze nsɛnkyerɛdze na anwanwadze, na nsa a ɔyɛ dzen, na basa a atsen, na ehudze kɛse, yii wo man Israel fii Egypt asaase do;
    19. na emaa hɔn asaase yi a ekaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hɔn egyanom dɛ edze bɛma hɔn no, asaase a ɔpem numfonsu na ewo;
    20. na wɔbae bɛfae dzii, na woenntsie wo ndze, eso wɔannantsew wo mbra do; wɔannyɛ dza ehyɛɛ hɔn dɛ wɔnyɛ no nyinara mu biara: dɛm ntsi na ama mbusu yi nyina aba hɔn do yi:
    21. hwɛ, mpempe no wɔaba kurow no ho dɛ wɔrebɛgye; na wɔdze kurow no ahyɛ Kaldeafo a wɔnye no roko nsa, na afona, na ɔkɔm, na ɔyardɔm no ntsi na dza ekae no aba mu; na hwɛ w'enyi tua.
    22. Na ɔwo, EWURADZE Nyankopɔn, esee me dɛ, Fa dwɛɛtɛɛ tɔ mfuwa no, na frɛ ho adasefo; na eso na kurow no wɔdze ahyɛ Kaldeafo nsa.
    23. Nna EWURADZE n'asɛm baa Jeremia hɔ, dɛ, JER.32.27, Hwɛ, emi nye EWURADZE, adasa nyinara Nyankopɔn: aso biribiara wɔ hɔ a ɔyɛ dzen ma me?
    24. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Hwɛ, medze kurow yi bɛhyɛ Kaldeafo nsa, na Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar nsa, ma ɔagye:
    25. na Kaldeafo a wɔnye kurow yi roko no, wɔbɛba abɔto kurow yi mu ogya, na wɔahyew no, ɔnye efiefi a wɔahyehyew n'etsifi nduhuam ama Baal, na woehue ɔnom afɔr ama abosom afofor, dɛ wɔdze riyi me ebufuw no.
    26. Na Israelmba na Judamba wɔayɛ dza ɔyɛ mbusu ara wɔ m'enyim ofir hɔn mbofraber mu: na Israelmba wɔdze hɔn nsaano edwuma eyi me ebufuw ara, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    27. Na kurow yi eyi me ebufuw na ebufuhyew ara ofi da a wɔkyekyeree dze bodu ndɛ da yi mpo; ma meeyi no efi m'enyi do:
    28. wɔ Israelmba na Judamba hɔn mbusu nyinara a wɔabɔ dze eyi me ebufuw no ntsi hɔn, hɔn ahemfo, hɔn mbapɔmba hɔn asɔfoe, na hɔn nkɔnhyɛfo, na Juda mbarimba, na Jerusalɛm atsefo
    29. Na wɔadandan hɔn ekyir ama me, na nnyɛ hɔn enyim a: na kaansa makyerɛkyerɛ hɔn, mosoɛr ahema na mekyerɛkyerɛ hɔn mpo a, woenntsie dɛ wɔbɛgye nkyerɛkyerɛ.
    30. Na wɔdze hɔn ekyiwadze sisii ofi a wɔdze me dzin ato no no mu, dɛ wongu ho fi., #2 Ahe 23.10; Jer 7.30
    31. Na wosisii Baal no nsorɔnsorɔmbea a ɔwɔ Hinom bɔnsa no mu, dɛ wɔremma hɔn mbabanyin na hɔn mbabaa edua ogya mu ama Molek a nnyɛ emi na mehyɛɛ hɔn no mu, eso wɔammba m'adwen mu, dɛ wɔyɛ dɛm ekyiwadze yi; ma Juda aayɛ bɔn.
    32. Na afei dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn, se wɔ kurow yi a hom ka wɔ ho dɛ, Wɔdze ahyɛ Babilɔnhen ne nsa, wɔ afona, na ɔkɔm, na ɔyardɔm mu no ho nye yi:
    33. hwɛ, emi mara mobɔboa hɔn ano mefi asaase nyina a mapam hɔn makɔ do wɔ m'ebufuw, na m'ebufuhyew, na m'enyiber kɛse mu no; na medze hɔn bɛsan aba bea yi do bio, na mama wɔatsena dwudwoodwo:
    34. na wɔbɛyɛ me man, na emi so mayɛ hɔn Nyankopɔn:
    35. na mebɛma hɔn akoma kor na ɔkwan kor, ama woeesuro me afebɔɔ; wɔ hɔnara na hɔn mba a wobedzi hɔn ekyir hɔn yie ntsi:
    36. na mirinngyaa hɔn ekyir dzi, dɛ mebɛyɛ hɔn yie; na medze mo suro bɛhyɛ hɔn akoma mu, mma woeemmfi me nkyɛn annkɔ.
    37. Ampaara, m'enyi bɛgye hɔn ho dɛ mebɛyɛ hɔn yie, na medze m'akoma nyina na me kra nyina matsɛw hɔn asaase yi do nokwar mu.
    38. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Dɛ mbrɛ medze mbusu kɛse yi nyinara maba ɔman yi do no, dɛmara so na medze yie a mabɔ hɔn ho anohoba nyina mebɛba hɔn do.
    39. Na wɔbɔtotɔ mfuwa wɔ asaase yi a hom ka wɔ ho dɛ, Ɔyɛ amamfo, nyimpa anaa abowa nnyi do; wɔdze ahyɛ Kaldeafo nsa no mu.
    40. Nkorɔfo dze sika bɔtotɔ mfuwa, na wɔdze hɔn nsa ahyehyɛ nwoma ase na wɔasosɔw ano, na wɔafrɛfrɛ adasefo, wɔ Benjamin asaase do, na mbeambea a etwa Jerusalɛm ho ehyia, na Juda nkurow mu, na koko do nkurow mu, na ɔbɔnmu nkurow mu, na Pomu afamu nkurow mu: na medze hɔn ndɔmmum mebɛsan maba, EWURADZE na ɔse.

    Tsir 33

    1. EWURADZE n'asɛm baa Jeremia nkyɛn a otsia ebien, ber a ɔda ho da efiadze wɔ ɔweɔmfo abangua mu hɔ no, dɛ, JER.33.2, Mbrɛ EWURADZE a ɔyɛ adze yi, EWURADZE a ɔhyehyɛ ma otsim hɔ no; ne dzin dze EWURADZE no, ɔse nye yi:
    2. Frɛ me, na mebɛgye wo do, na makyerɛ wo ndzɛmba akɛse a ɔyɛ yɛ na a ɔwo innyim.
    3. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn, ɔse wɔ kurow yi mu adan, na Juda ahemfo adan a mpempe na afona ntsi woedwuruw egu famu no ho nye yi:
    4. Wɔreba wɔnye Kaldeafo abɔko, na mbom wɔdze nyimpa a mekuku hɔn wɔ m'ebufuw na m'ebufuhyew mu, na osian hɔn emumuyɛ nyinara ntsi ma medze m'enyim ehuntsa efi kurow yi ho no, hɔn efun abɛhyehyɛ no amaama.
    5. Hwɛ, emi mara mebɛbrɛ no apɔwmudzen na edur, na masa hɔn yarba; na meyi asomdwee na nokwar pii makyerɛ hɔn.
    6. Na mebɛma Juda ndɔmmum na Israel asan aba, na medze hɔn mesi hɔ dɛ asɔpɔn no.
    7. Na mebɛtsew hɔn ho efi hɔn emumuyɛ nyina a wɔdze ayɛ bɔn etsia me no ho; na medze hɔn emumuyɛ nyina a wɔdze ayɛ bɔn etsia me no, na wɔdze afom me no mefir hɔn.
    8. Na kurow yi bɛdan me ahosɛpɛw dzin, ayɛyi na enyimnyam wɔ asaase do amanaman nyina a wɔbɛtse yie a medze reyɛ hɔn no nyina enyim, na woesuro na hɔn ho apopo wɔ yie nyina na asomdwee nyina a mirinya mama hɔn no ntsi.
    9. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Bea yi a hom ka wɔ ho dɛ, Ɔayɛ amamfo, nyimpa na abowa biara nnyi hɔ, Juda nkurow mu mpo, Jerusalɛm abrɔn a ɔayɛ afo, nyimpa na tsefo na abowa biara nnyi mu no, na wɔbɛda ho atse
    10. ehurusi ndze na ahosɛpɛw ndze, na ayeforkun ndze na ayefor ndze, hɔn a wɔtow ndwom, ber a wɔdze ndaase afɔrbɔ reba EWURADZE fie no ndze dɛ, Hom mfa ndaase mma dɔm EWURADZE, na EWURADZE ye, na n'ehumbɔbɔr tsim hɔ daa, Na mebɛma asaase no asan ayɛ prɔmprɔm dɛ asɔpɔn no, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    11. Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE se nye yi: Bea yi a ɔabɔ a nyimpa na abowa biara nnyi, na no nkurow nyinara mu, ɔbɛyɛ tsenabea bio ama nguanhwɛfo a wɔbɛma hɔn nguan ebutubutuw hɔ.
    12. Koko do nkurow, bɔnsamu nkurow, na Pomu afamu nkurow, na Benjamin asaase do, na mbeambea a etwa Jerusalɛm ho ehyia, na Juda nkurow mu, na nguankuw bodua nyia ɔkan hɔn no nsa ase etwa mu bio, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    13. Hwɛ, nda reba a, EWURADZE na ɔse, mebɛma asɛmpa no a mekaa no Israel fifo ho na Juda fifo ho no aba mu., #Jer 23.5
    14. Nda no mu no, na aber no, nna mebɛma ɔtsenenee Odubaa afefɛw ama David; na ɔayɛ atsɛmbu na tsenenee wɔ asaase no do.
    15. Nda no mu na Jerusalɛm atsena ase dwudwoodwo: na iyi nye dzin a wɔdze bɛfrɛ no, EWURADZE nye hɛn tsenenee.
    16. Na mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Ɔbarimba a ɔbɛtsena Israel fie akɔngua do ɔrommbɔ David;
    17. eso ɔbarimba a ɔbɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr, na ɔahyew edziban afɔr, na ɔabɔ okum afɔr daapem wɔ m'enyim no, ɔrommbɔ asɔfo Levifo no.
    18. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa Jeremia hɔ, dɛ, JER.33.20, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Sɛ hom botum ato m'adzekyee ahyɛmu na m'adzesaa ahyɛmu, ma adzekyee na adzesaa remmba bio wɔ n'aber mu a;
    19. ɔnodze na wɔbɔto menye m'akowaa David ntamu ahyɛmu no, ma onnkenya ɔbabanyin a ɔbɛtsena n'akɔngua do edzi hen; na ɔnye Levifo asɔfo a wɔsom me no.
    20. Dɛ mbrɛ wonntum nnkan ɔsor dɔm, eso wonnsusu mpoano anhwea no; dɛmara na mebɛma m'akowaa David asefo, na Levifo a wɔsom me no wɔadɔr.
    21. Na EWURADZE n'asɛm baa Jeremia hɔ, dɛ, JER.33.24, Ana enndwen dza ɔman yi aka no ho, dɛ, Mbusu ebien a EWURADZE saan mu yii hɔn no, wɔatow hɔn akyen? Mbrɛ wobu me man enyimtsia nye yi, dɛ wɔnnyɛ hɔn enyi do dɛ ɔman bio.
    22. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Sɛ m'adzekyee na adzesaa ahyɛmu no enngyina a, sɛ mannhyɛ ɔsor na asaase ahyɛdze no a;
    23. ɔnodze na mo so mobɔtow Jakob, na m'akowaa David asefo akyen, dɛ mennkɛfa n'asefo mu bi ma woeedzi Abraham, Isaak, na Jakob asefo do mpanyin: na mebɛma hɔn ndɔmmumfo asan, na mehu hɔn mbɔbɔr.

    Tsir 34

    1. Asɛm a ofi EWURADZE nkyɛn baa Jeremia hɔ, aber a Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar, na no dɔm nyina, na asaase do ahendzi a wɔwɔ no tumdzi ase nyina, na aman nyina, bɛnye Jerusalɛm, na no nkurow nyinara koe dɛ:
    2. Mbrɛ EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn, se nye yi, Kɔ kɛkasa kyerɛ Judahen Zedekia, na se no dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Hwɛ, medze kurow yi bɛhyɛ Babilɔnhen nsa, na ɔdze ogya ahyew no:
    3. na ɔwoara so irimmfi ne nsa, na ɔkyer ara na wɔbɛkyer wo, na woeyi wo ahyɛ ne nsa; na w'enyiwa bohu Babilɔnhen enyi, na ɔnye wo akasa ano na ano, na akɔ Babilɔn.
    4. Naaso Judahen Zedekia, tsie EWURADZE n'asɛm: mbrɛ EWURADZE ka wɔ wo ho nye yi, Innkowu afona ano;
    5. ibowu asomdwee mu; na mbrɛ wɔhyehyeew adze maa w'egyanom, ahemfo nkankan no a wodzii w'enyim no, dɛmara so na wɔbɛhyew ama wo; na wobegyam wo, dɛ, Ao ewura! Na emi na maka asɛm no, EWURADZE na ɔse.
    6. Nna nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia kaa nsɛm yinom nyina kyerɛɛ Judahen Zedekia wɔ Jerusalɛm, JER.34.7, ber a Babilɔnhen no dɔm wɔnye Jerusalɛm, na Juda nkurow a aka no, Lakis na Azeka, ridzi ako no; na iyinom nye nkurow a wɔagye ho ban a wɔkae wɔ Juda nkurow no mu.
    7. Asɛm a ofi EWURADZE nkyɛn baa Jeremia hɔ, aber a ɔhen Zedekia nye nkorɔfo a wɔwɔ Jerusalɛm nyinara dzii ahyɛmu no dɛ wɔmbɔ fahodzi dawur mma hɔn no ekyir no;
    8. dɛ nyimpa biara mma n'akowaa, na nyimpa biara mma n'afonabaa a ɔyɛ Hebriwnyi banyin anaa Hebriwnyi basia mmfa noho ndzi; dɛ mma biara nndzi hɔn nya, mekyerɛ, no nua Hebriwnyi no a:
    9. na asafohen no nyinara na ɔman no nyinara a wodzii ahyɛmu no tsiei, dɛ biara mma n'akowaa, na biara mma n'afonabaa mfa noho ndzi, na mma biara nndzi hɔn nya bio; wotsiei na wɔmaa wɔfaa hɔnho dzii;
    10. na n'ekyir no wotwaa hɔnho, na wɔmaa nkowaa na mfonabaa a wɔama wɔafa hɔnho edzi no, sanee bae bɛyɛɛ nkowaa na mfonabaa bio.
    11. Dɛm ntsi EWURADZE n'asɛm fi EWURADZE nkyɛn baa Jeremia hɔ, dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn se nye yi:
    12. Menye hom egyanom dzii ahyɛmu wɔ da a medze hɔn mifii Egypt asaase do, fii nkowaasom fi no mu no, dɛ, JER.34.14, Mfe esuon ewiei no, hom mu nyimpa biara mma no nua a ɔyɛ Hebriwnyi a wɔatɔn no ama wo no, na ɔasom wo mfe esia no, ɔnkɔ nkɛfa noho ndzi mfi wo nkyɛn: na hom egyanom enntsie me, eso wɔammbrɛ hɔn aso adze.
    13. Na hom dze, ndaenu yi hom sanee, na hom yɛɛ dza ɔtsen wɔ m'enyi do, dɛ hom mu nyimpa biara bɔɔ fahodzi dawur maa ne nyɛnko; na hom enya edzi ahyɛmu wɔ m'enyim wɔ fi a wɔdze me dzin ato no no mu:
    14. na hom sanee boguu me dzin ho fi, na hom maa nyimpa biara n'akowaa, na nyimpa biara n'afonabaa a hom maa wɔfaa hɔnho dzii dɛ mbrɛ wɔpɛ no, sanee bae; na hom tseetsee hɔn dɛ nkowaa na mfonabaa.
    15. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Hom enntsie me dɛ hom bɔbɔ fahodzi dawur, nyimpa biara dze ama no nua, na nyimpa biara dze ama ne nyɛnko: hwɛ, mo so morobɔ fahodzi dawur, EWURADZE na ɔse, medze hom mama afona, ɔyardɔm, na ɔkɔm; na mebɛma wɔatow hom edzi akɔnaaba wɔ asaase do ahendzi horow nyina mu.
    16. Na medze mbarimba a wɔato m'ahyɛmu, wɔannyɛ ahyɛmu a wodzii no m'enyim no mu nsɛm no, ber a wɔpaa ɔnantwiba mu ebien no, ha woduaa n'afaafa no ntamu no;
    17. Juda asafohen, na Jerusalɛm asafohen, epiafo no, na asɔfo no, na asaase no do nkorɔfo no nyinara a woduaa ɔnantwiba n'afaafa ntamu no;
    18. ɔhyɛ ara na medze hɔn mebɛhyɛ hɔn atamfo nsa, na hɔn a wɔhwehwɛ hɔn nkwa no nsa: na hɔn efun bɛyɛ edziban ama sor nnoma, na asaase mbowa.
    19. Na Judahen Zedekia na n'asafohen no so medze hɔn mebɛhyɛ hɔn atamfo nsa, na hɔn a wɔhwehwɛ hɔn nkwa nsa na Babilɔnhen no dɔm a woefi hom enyim kɔ no nsa.
    20. Hwɛ, mebɛhyɛ, EWURADZE na ɔse, na mama wɔasan aba kurow yi ho; na wɔnye no bɔko, na wɔagye, na wɔdze gya ahyew no: na mebɛyɛ Juda nkurow amamfo a ɔtsefo nnyi mu.

    Tsir 35

    1. Asɛm a ofi EWURADZE nkyɛn baa Jeremia hɔ wɔ Judahen Josia ne ba Jehoiakim ne nda no mu dɛ
    2. Kɔ Rekabfo fie, na kɛkasa kyerɛ hɔn, na fa hɔn bra EWURADZE fie mpia no kor mu, na ma hɔn nsa ma wɔnnom.
    3. Nna mefaa Habazinia ba Jeremia ne ba Jaazania, na no nuanom, na ne mbabanyin nyinara, na Rekabfo fie nyinara;
    4. na medze hɔn mebaa EWURADZE fie, wɔ Nyame nyimpa Igdalia ba Hanan ne mbabanyin hɔn pia no a ɔwɔ abowanohwɛfo Sallum ba Maaseia ne pia etsifi no mu:
    5. na medze kuraba a nsa ahyehyɛ no amaama, na nkɔɔpow sisii hɔn enyim, na mesee hɔn dɛ, Hom nnom nsa ɛ.
    6. Na wɔkaa dɛ, Yɛnnkɔnom nsa biara: na hɛn egya Rekab ne ba Jonadab hyɛɛ hɛn, dɛ, Hom o, hom mbabanyin o, mma hom nnom nsa dabiarada:
    7. eso mma hom nnsi dan, na wonndua aba, anaa wɔnntsɛw wenyin ture, anaa wonnya bi: na mbom hom ntsena asese mu hom nda nyina; ama hom aatsena ase nda pii wɔ asaase a hom yɛ do amamforafo no mu.
    8. Na yɛayɛ setsie ama hɛn egya Rekab ne ba Jonadab wɔ dza ɔdze hyɛɛ hɛn nyinara ho dɛ, mma yɛnnom nsa hɛn nda nyinara, hɛnara, hɛn yernom, hɛn mbabanyin, na hɛn mbabaa;
    9. anaaso yennsisi adan yɛnntsena mu: eso yennyi wenyin ture, na mfuwa, na aba:
    10. mbom yɛatsenatsena asese mu, na yɛayɛ setsie, na yɛayɛ dɛ mbrɛ hɛn egya Jonadab hyɛɛ hɛn no nyinara.
    11. Na ɔbaa dɛ, ber a Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar tui baa asaase yi do no, nna yɛsee dɛ, Hom mbra ma yɛnkɔ Jerusalɛm wɔ Kaldeafo dɔm ho hu ntsi, na Siriafo dɔm ho hu ntsi; nna yɛtse Jerusalɛm yi.
    12. Nna EWURADZE n'asɛm baa Jeremia hɔ, dɛ, JER.35.13, Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn, se nye yi: Kɔ, na kɛse Juda mbarimba na Jerusalɛm atsefo dɛ, Aso hom nnkɛgye nkyerɛkyerɛ dɛ hom betsie me nsɛm bi a? EWURADZE na ɔse.
    13. Nsɛm a Rekab ba Jonadab dze hyɛɛ ne mbabanyin dɛ mma wɔnnom nsa no, woedzi do, na ɔdze bodu ndɛ da yi wɔnnoom bi, osiandɛ wodzi hɔn egya ne mbrasɛm do: na emi dze, makasa makyerɛ hom, mosoɛr ahema na mekasa; na hom enntsie me.
    14. Masoma mo nkowaa nkɔnhyɛfo no nyinara aba hom nkyɛn, eso mosoɛr ahema na mosoma hɔn, dɛ, Afei hom mu nyimpa biara nsan mfi no kwan bɔn no do, na ɔnyɛ ne nyɛe yie, na mma onnkedzi abosom afofor bi ekyir nnkɔsom hɔn, na hom atsena asaase a medze mama hom na hom egyanom no do: na mbom hom ammbrɛ hom aso adze, eso hom enntsie me.
    15. Susuampaara dɛ Rekab na Jonadab ne mba woedzi mbrasɛm a hɔn egya dze hyɛɛ hɔn no do no, na ɔman yi dze, woenntsie me yi;
    16. dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE, dɔm Nyankopɔn, Israel Nyankopɔn, ɔse nye yi: Hwɛ, medze mbusu nyina a maka etsia Juda na Jerusalɛm atsefo nyinara no mebɛba hɔn do: osiandɛ makasa akyerɛ hɔn, na woenntsie; mafrɛ hɔn so, na wɔanngye do.
    17. Na Jeremia see Rekabfo fi no dɛ, Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn, se nye yi: Osiandɛ hom etsie hom egya Jonadab ne mbrasɛm, na hom edzi n'ahyɛdze nyinara do, na hom ayɛ dɛ mbrɛ ɔhyɛɛ hom nyinara ntsi;
    18. dɛm ntsi mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn, se nye yi: Ɔbarimba a ogyina m'enyim nnkɔbɔ Rekab ba Jonadab ara da.

    Tsir 36

    1. Na ɔbaa dɛ Josia ba Jehoiakim, Judahen no, n'afe a otsia anan no mu no nna asɛm yi fi EWURADZE nkyɛn baa Jeremia hɔ, dɛ, , #2 Ahe 24.1; 2 Mbe 36.5-7; Dan 1.1
    2. Fa nwoma mbobɔwee, na kyerɛw nsɛm nyina a maka akyerɛ wo etsia Israel, na Juda, na amanaman nyina wɔ mu, ofi da a mekasaa kyerɛɛ wo fi Josia ber do dze besi ndɛ da yi mpo.
    3. Bi a Juda fi bɛtse mbusu nyina a mesua me tsir mu dɛ medze bɛyɛ hɔn; ama hɔn mu nyimpa biara ɔaasan efi no kwan bɔn do; ama medze hɔn emumuyɛ na hɔn bɔn aakyɛ hɔn.
    4. Nna Jeremia frɛɛ Neria ba Baruk; na Baruk kyerɛɛw EWURADZE nsɛm a ɔkaa kyerɛɛ Jeremia nyina fir n'anomu hyɛɛ nwoma mbobɔwee no mu.
    5. Na Jeremia hyɛɛ Baruk, dɛ, Wɔatow me mu; murunntum nnkɔ EWURADZE fie:
    6. Dɛm ntsi ɔwoara kɔ, na kɛkenkan EWURADZE nsɛm a ekyerɛwee no, wɔ EWURADZE fie, wɔ mbuadadzi da no mu: na kenkan no wɔ Judafo nyina a wofi hɔn nkurow do ba no so asomu.
    7. Bi a wɔdze hɔn nkotoserɛ bogu EWURADZE enyim, na hɔn mu biara bɛsan efi no kwan bɔn no do: na ebufuw na ebufuhyew a EWURADZE aka egu ɔman yi do no ɔso.
    8. Na Neria ba Baruk yɛɛ dɛ dza nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia hyɛɛ no no nyina, na ɔkenkaan EWURADZE nsɛm no a ɔwɔ nwoma no mu no wɔ EWURADZE fie.
    9. Afei ɔbaa dɛ Josua ba Jehoiakim, Judahen no, n'afe a otsia enum no, wɔ bosoom a otsia akron no, nkorɔfo a wɔwɔ Jerusalɛm nyina, na nkorɔfo a wofi Juda mu baa Jerusalɛm nyina, wɔbɔɔ mbuadadzi ho dawur wɔ EWURADZE enyim.
    10. Nna Baruk kenkaan Jeremia ne nsɛm a ɔwɔ nwoma no mu no wɔ EWURADZE fie, wɔ ɔkyerɛwfo Safan ne ba Gemaria ne pia a ɔwɔ etsifi abangua no mu wɔ EWURADZE fie ɔponkɛse no ano, wɔ ɔman no nyina asomu.
    11. Na Safan ne ba Gemaria ne babanyin Mikaia tsee EWURADZE nsɛm a ɔwɔ nwoma no mu no nyina no, JER.36.12, osianee kɔr ɔhen ne fie. Ɔkɔr ɔkyerɛwfo no ne pia no mu: na, hwɛ, asafohen no nyina tsetse hɔ, mekyerɛ ɔkyerɛwfo Elisama, na Semaia ba Delaia, na Akbor ba Elnatan, na Safan ba Gemaria, na Hanania ba Zedekia, na asafohen no nyinara.
    12. Nna Mikaia kaa nsɛm a ɔtsee no ber a Baruk kenkaan nwoma no wɔ ɔman no asomu nyina kyerɛɛ hɔn.
    13. Dɛm ntsi asafohen no somaa Jehudi a ofi Kusi ebusua mu no wɔ Baruk hɔ, dɛ, Fa nwoma mbobɔwee no a akenkan mu nsɛm wɔ ɔman no asomu no kitsa wo nsamu bra. Nna Neria ba Baruk faa nwoma mbobɔwee no kitsaa ne nsamu na ɔbaa hɔn nkyɛn.
    14. Na wɔsee no dɛ, Tsena ase ɛ, na kenkan no hɛn asomu. Nna Baruk kenkaan no hɔn asomu.
    15. Afei ɔbaa dɛ, wonyae tsee nsɛm no nyinara no, wɔdze akomatu danee hwehwɛɛ hɔnho, na wɔsee Baruk dɛ, Otwar dɛ yɛkɛka nsɛm yi nyina kyerɛ ɔhen.
    16. Na wobisaa Baruk dɛ, Afei ka kyerɛ hɛn, Isii dɛn kyerɛɛw nsɛm yi nyina? Ana ɔkae ma ekyerɛwee a?
    17. Nna Baruk buaa hɔn dɛ, Ɔdze n'ano kaa nsɛm yi nyinara kyerɛɛ me, na mo so medze dubir kyerɛwee guu nwoma mu.
    18. Nna asafohen no see Baruk dɛ, Kɔ, kosuma, ɔwo na Jeremia; mma obiara nnhu mbrɛ hom wɔ.
    19. Asafohen no dze nwoma mbobɔwee no siee ɔkyerɛwfo Elisama ne pia no mu; na wɔkɔr ɔhen no nkyɛn wɔ abangua no do; na wɔkaa nsɛm no nyina wɔ ɔhen no asomu.
    20. Nna ɔhen no somaa Jehudi dɛ ɔnkɛfa nwoma mbobɔwee no mbra: na okeyii no ɔkyerɛwfo Elisama ne pia no mu. Na Jehudi kenkanee kyerɛɛ ɔhen no na asafohen a wogyinagyina ɔhen no nkyɛn nyinara.
    21. Nna ɔhen tse awɔwber dan no mu, wɔ bosoom a otsia akron no mu: na mbukyia mu ogya a ɔredzɛw taa n'enyim.
    22. Na ɔbaa dɛ, aber a Jehudi wiee nkrataa ebiasa anaa anan kenkan no, ɔhen no dze sekamba twitwae na ɔdze guu gya a ɔwɔ mbukyia mu no mu kesii dɛ nwoma mbobɔwee no nyina hyewee wɔ ogya a ɔwɔ mbukyia mu no.
    23. Na woennsuro, eso woennsunsuan hɔn ntar mu, ɔhen no, na no nkowaa nyinara.
    24. Mpo ber a Elnatan na Delaia na Gemaria totɔe serɛɛ ɔhen no dɛ nkyɛ mma ɔnnhyew nwoma mbobɔwee no: oenntsie hɔn.
    25. Na ɔhen no hyɛɛ ɔhenba Jerameel, na Azriel ba Seraia, na Abdeel ba Selemia, dɛ wɔnkɛkyer ɔkyerɛwfo Baruk na nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia: naaso EWURADZE dze hɔn sumae.
    26. Afei ɔhen no hyeew nwoma mbobɔwee no a nsɛm a Baruk kyerɛwee fii Jeremia anomu wɔ mu no ekyir no, EWURADZE n'asɛm baa Jeremia hɔ, dɛ, JER.36.28, Fa nwoma mbobɔwee fofor so bio, na kyerɛw nkan nsɛm a ɔwɔ nwoma mbobɔwee a odzi kan no a Judahen Jehoiakim ahyew no no, wɔ mu.
    27. Na ka wɔ Judahen Jehoiakim ho dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Ɔwo ahyew nwoma mbobɔwee yi, na ase dɛ, Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na akyerɛw no wɔ mu dɛ, Babilɔnhen bɛba abɛsɛɛ asaase yi ampaara, na ɔama nyimpa na abowa abɔ adze wɔ do?
    28. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ EWURADZE ka wɔ Judahen Jehoiakim ho nye yi: Onnkenya obi a ɔbɛtsena David akɔngua do: na no fun so wɔbɔtow akyen ma ɔhyew afa do ewiaber, na awɔw afa do anadwe.
    29. Na mebɛtsea ɔno na n'asefo na no nkowaa wɔ hɔn emumuyɛ ntsi, na medze mbusu nyina a maka etsia hɔn no, na woenntsie no, bɛba hɔn na Jerusalɛm nyina, na Judamba do.
    30. Nna Jeremia faa nwoma mbobɔwee fofor so, na ɔdze maa ɔkyerɛwfo Baruk, Neria ba no ɔno na ɔkyerɛɛw nwoma a Judahen Jehoiakim hyeew no wɔ gya mu no no mu nsɛm nyina fii Jeremia anomu hyɛɛ mu: na wɔdze nsɛm a ɔtsetse dɛm pii kekaa ho.

    Tsir 37

    1. Na Josia ba Zedekia dzii hen wɔ Jehoiakim ba Konia a Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar hyɛɛ no hen wɔ Juda asaase no do no ananmu.
    2. Na ɔno o, no nkowaa o, asaase no do nkorɔfo o, woenntsie EWURADZE ne nsɛm a ɔnam nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia do kae no.
    3. Na ɔhen Zedekia somaa Selemia ba Jehukal, na ɔsɔfo Zefania, Maaseia ne ba no wɔ nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia nkyɛn, dɛ, Afei yi mpaa ma EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn ma hɛn.
    4. Nna Jeremia dzi ɔman no mu ndɔfir: osiandɛ nna wonnyae mmfaa no nntoo efiadze.
    5. Ber no nna Farao no dɔm efir edzi fi Egypt reba: na ber a Kaldeafo a wobotuaa Jerusalɛm no tsee hɔn nka no, wotui fii Jerusalɛm.
    6. Nna EWURADZE nsɛm baa nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia hɔ, dɛ, JER.37.7, Mbrɛ EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn no, ɔse nye yi: Mbrɛ hom nkɛse Judahen a ɔsomaa hom me nkyɛn dɛ hom mbebisa mo hɔ adze no, nye yi. Hwɛ, Farao no dɔm a woefir edzi robɔboa hom no, wɔbɛsan akɔ Egypt hɔnankasa hɔn asaase do.
    7. Na Kaldeafo no bɛba bio, na wɔnye kurow yi abɔko, na wɔbɛgye na wɔdze gya ahyew no.
    8. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi: Mma hom nndaadaa homho, dɛ, Ɔkɔ ara na Kaldeafo befi hɛn nkyɛn akɔ: osiandɛ wɔronnkɔ.
    9. Na kaansa hom kuku Kaldeafo dɔm a wɔnye hom roko nyina, na ɔka hɔn mu epirafo nko mpo a, nkyɛ hɔn mu nyimpa biara bɔsoɛr efi n'asesee mu, na wɔdze gya ahyew kurow yi.
    10. Na ɔbaa dɛ Kaldeafo dɔm tui fii Jerusalɛm wɔ Farao no dɔm ho hu ntsi no, JER.37.12, nna Jeremia fii Jerusalɛm dɛ ɔrokɔ Benjamin asaase do akɛgye ne kyɛfa wɔ hɔ wɔ ɔman no ne finimfin.
    11. Na odur Benjamin ɔponkɛse no mu no, na aweɔmfo panyin bi wɔ hɔ a ne dzin dze Irija, Hanania ba Selemia ne ba a; na osuoo nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia mu, see dɛ, Ɔwo adan rokɔ Kaldeafo nkyɛn.
    12. Nna Jeremia see dɛ, Eboa; mennyɛ nyia ɔadan rokɔ Kaldeafo nkyɛn; naaso oenntsie no: nna Irija suoo Jeremia mu, na ɔdze no brɛɛ asafohen no.
    13. Na asafohen no bo fuuw Jeremia, na wɔhwee no, na wɔdze no kɔtoo efiadze wɔ ɔkyerɛwfo Jonatan fie; nna hɔ na wɔdze ayɛ efiadze.
    14. Na Jeremia kɔr mona efiadze no mu, na etu no mu, na Jeremia dzii hɔ nda pii.
    15. Nna ɔhen Zedekia somae ma wɔkɛfaa no bae: na ɔhen no bisaa no wɔ ne fie nsumaa mu, dɛ, Ana asɛm bi a ofi EWURADZE nkyɛn wɔ hɔ? Na Jeremia see dɛ, Bi wɔ hɔ. Ɔkae so dɛ, Wobeyi wo ahyɛ Babilɔnhen ne nsa.
    16. Bio so Jeremia see ɔhen Zedekia dɛ, Ebɛnadze mu na mayɛ bɔn etsia ɔwo, anaa wo nkowaa, anaa wo man, ma hom dze me ato efiadze yi?
    17. Hom nkɔnhyɛfo a wɔhyɛɛ hom nkɔm dɛ, Babilɔnhen remmba hom do, anaa asaase yi do no, wɔwɔ henfa?
    18. Na afei, mo wura ɔhen, meserɛ wo, tsie ɛ: meserɛ wo ma mo nkotoserɛ nsɔ w'enyi; na mma wɔmmfa me nnsan ɔkyerɛwfo Jonatan fie, ɔno bɛyɛ na mewu wɔ hɔ.
    19. Nna ɔhen Zedekia hyɛe ma wɔdze Jeremia kesiee aweɔmfo abangua no mu, ma daa wofi boodootofo brɔn no mu ma no boodoo ntɔwmu kor, dze kodur dɛ kurow no mu boodoo nyina sae. Mbrɛ Jeremia tsenaa aweɔmfo abangua no mu nye no.

    Tsir 38

    1. Na Maatan ba Sefatia, na Pasur ba Gedalia, na Selemia ba Jukal, na Malkia ba Pasur tsee nsɛm a Jeremia kaa kyerɛɛ ɔman no nyina, dɛ, JER.38.2, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Nyia ɔbɛtsena kurow yi mu no, obowu afona, ɔkɔm, na ɔyardɔm ano: na nyia obefir edzi akɔ Kaldeafo nkyɛn no dze, ɔbɛtsena ase, na no nkwa bɛyɛ no dɛ afonam, na ɔbɛtsena ase.
    2. Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Wɔdze kurow yi bɛhyɛ Babilɔnhen no dɔm nsa ara ampa, na wɔagye.
    3. Nna asafohen no see ɔhen no dɛ, Yɛserɛ wo, Ma wonku ɔbarimba yi: susuampaara dɛ ɔgow akofo a wɔaka wɔ kurow yi mu nsa, na ɔman no nyinara nsa, wɔ dɛ ɔka dɛm nsɛm yi kyerɛ hɔn ntsi: na ɔbarimba yi ɔnnhwehwɛ ɔman yi ne yie, na mbom no mbusu a.
    4. Na ɔhen Zedekia see dɛ, Hwɛ, ɔwɔ hom nsamu: na nnyɛ ɔhen nye nyia obotum ayɛ biribi etsia hom.
    5. Nna wɔfaa Jeremia, na wɔkotoow no kyeen ɔhenba Malkia mona efiadze a ɔwɔ aweɔmfo abanguado no mu: na wɔdze ntampehoma gyaagyaa Jeremia siaan mu. Na mona efiadze no hɔ nnyi nsu, dɛ adɛtsebir nko: na Jeremia homee kɔr adɛtsebir no mu.
    6. Afei ber a Etiopianyi Ebed-melek, opianyi a ɔwɔ ahemfie no, tsee dɛ wɔdze Jeremia akɔto mona efiadze no, nna ɔhen no so tse Benjamin ɔponkɛse mu no, JER.38.8, Ebed-melek fiir edzi fii ahemfie, kɛkasaa kyerɛɛ ɔhen no, dɛ, JER.38.9, Mo wura ɔhen, mbarimba yi abɔ mbusu wɔ dza wɔdze ayɛ nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia no nyina, dɛ wɔakɔtow no akyen mona efiadze no mu; na ɔkɔm ntsi ɔreyɛ oewu wɔ mbrɛ ɔwɔ no: osiandɛ edziban bi nnyi kurow no mu bio.
    7. Nna ɔhen no hyɛɛ Etiopianyi Ebed-melek, dɛ, Fa mbarimba eduasa fi ha ka wo ho, na keyi nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia fi mona efiadze no mu, ansaana oewu.
    8. Nna Ebed-melek faa mbarimba no kaa no ho, na ɔkɔr ahemfie adzekoradan no ase, na ɔkɛfaa ntangow dadaw a atsetsew na esusuw, na ɔdze ntampehoma kyekyeree gyaagyaa mu siaan mona efiadze no mu maa Jeremia.
    9. Na Etiopianyi Ebed-melek see Jeremia dɛ, Fa ntangow dadaw a atsetsew na esusuw no hyehyɛ w'ambɔtoadze wɔ ntampehoma no ase. Na Jeremia yɛɛ dɛm.
    10. Nna wɔdze ntampehoma no twee Jeremia baa sor, na woyii no fii mona efiadze no mu: na Jeremia tsenaa aweɔmfo abangua no mu.
    11. Nna ɔhen Zedekia somae ma wɔkɛfaa nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia baa ne nkyɛn wɔ EWURADZE fie abow a otsia ebiasa no ano: na ɔhen no see Jeremia dɛ, Miribebisa wo asɛm bi; na mma nnsiw me biribiara do.
    12. Nna Jeremia see Zedekia dɛ, Aso mepaa mu ka kyerɛ wo a, ana nnyɛ oku ara na woboku me bi? Na sɛ mema wo apam a, irinntsie me.
    13. Nna Zedekia kaa ntam nsumaa mu kyerɛɛ Jeremia, dɛ, Dɛ EWURADZE a ɔyɛɛ hɛn kra yi tse ase yi, murunnku wo, eso meremmfa wo nhyɛ mbarimba yi a wɔrohwehwɛ wo nkwa yi nsamu.
    14. Nna Jeremia see Zedekia dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE dɔm Nyankopɔn, Israel Nyankopɔn no, ɔse nye yi: Sɛ ibefir edzi akɔ Babilɔnhen n'asafohen no nkyɛn a, nkyɛ ɔnodze wo kra bɛtsena ase, na kurow yi so, wɔnnkɛfa gya ahyew no; na ɔwo na wo fifo bɛtsena ase:
    15. na sɛ irimmfi edzi nnkɔ Babilɔnhen n'asafohemfo no nkyɛn a, ɔnodze wɔdze kurow yi bɛhyɛ Kaldeafo nsa, na wɔdze gya ahyew no, na ɔwoara so irimmfi hɔn nsa mfi.
    16. Na ɔhen Zedekia see Jeremia dɛ, Musuro Judafo a wɔadan kɔ Kaldeafo no nkyɛn no, bi a wobeyi me ahyɛ hɔn nsa, na woesi me atwetwe.
    17. Na Jeremia see dɛ, Wonnkeyi wo ama. Meserɛ wo ara, tsie EWURADZE ne ndze wɔ dza mereka kyerɛ wo yi mu: dɛm na obesi wo yie, na wo kra atsena ase.
    18. Na sɛ epow dɛ ibefir edzi akɔ a, asɛm a EWURADZE dze akyerɛ me nye yi:
    19. Hwɛ, mbaa a wɔaka wɔ Judahen ne fie nyina wɔdze hɔn befir edzi akɔ Babilɔnhen n'asafohen no nkyɛn, na mbaa no bɛse dɛ, W'anyɛnko brɛbo na wɔadaadaa wo, na woedzi wo do nyim: afei a w'anan atɔ adɛtsebir mu yi, wɔadan wo egya.
    20. Na wɔdze wo yernom na wo mba nyinara befir edzi akɔ Kaldeafo nkyɛn: na ɔwoara nnkefi hɔn nsa efi, na mbom Babilɔnhen ne nsa bɛka wo: na ɔwoara na ebɛma wɔdze gya ahyew kurow yi.
    21. Nna Zedekia see Jeremia dɛ, Mma nyimpa biara nntse asɛm yi, na innkowu.
    22. Na iyi sɛ asafohen no tse dɛ menye wo akasa a, na wɔba wo nkyɛn, na wɔbɛse wo dɛ, Afei ka dza aka akyerɛ ɔhen no kyerɛ hɛn; mma nnsiw hɛn biribiara do, na yerunnku wo: eso dza ɔhen kaa kyerɛɛ wo no, a:
    23. ɔnodze se hɔn dɛ, Mo nkotoserɛ na medze koguu ɔhen no enyim, dɛ mma ɔmma me nnsan nnkɔ Jonatan fie munnkowu wɔ hɔ.
    24. Nna asafohen no nyinara baa Jeremia nkyɛn bebisaa no: na ɔkaa nsɛm yi a ɔhen no hyɛɛ no no nyinara kyerɛɛ hɔn dɛmara. Nna wogyaa dɛ wɔnye no kasa; osiandɛ woennhu asɛm no.
    25. Nna Jeremia tsenaa aweɔmfo abangua no mu ara dze kodur dɛ wɔgyee Jerusalɛm.

    Tsir 39

    1. Na ɔbaa dɛ wɔgyee Jerusalɛm (wɔ Judahen Zedekia afe a otsia akron no mu, bosoom du no mu no, Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar na no dɔm nyinara wɔbaa Jerusalɛm, na wobotuaa no;
    2. Zedekia afe a otsia dubiako no, bosoom a otsia anan no, na bosoom no mu da a otsia akron no mu, na wokefiir kurow no mu:)
    3. ma Babilɔnhen n'asafohen no nyinara bɛhɛɛn kurow no mu, na wɔtsenatsenaa finimfin abow kɛse no mu, mekyerɛ Nergal-sarezer, Samgar-nebo, Sarsekim, Rab-saris, Nergal-sarezer, Rab-mag, wɔnye Babilɔnhen n'asafohen nkaa no nyinara.
    4. Na ɔbaa dɛ aber a Judahen Zedekia, na mbarimba akofo no nyinara hun hɔn no, nna woguanguanee, na wofii kurow no mu fiir anadwe, duaa ɔhen no ture mu kwan do, dze faa abow kɛse mu wɔ afasu ebien ntamu: na wɔdze faa Araba kwan do kɔree.
    5. Na Kaldeafo hɔn dɔm no tsiiw hɔn, na wɔkɔtoo Zedekia wɔ Jeriko tɛtɛr mu: na wɔkyeer no no, wɔdze no baa Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar nkyɛn wɔ Ribla wɔ Hamat asaase do, na obuaa no atsɛn.
    6. Nna Babilɔnhen kunkum Zedekia ne mba wɔ Ribla wɔ n'enyim: eso Babilɔnhen kunkum Juda ekunyin no nyinara.
    7. Afei so otutuu Zedekia n'enyiwa, na ɔtoo no mpokyerɛ dɛ wɔmfa no nkɔ Babilɔn.
    8. Na Kaldeafo dze gya hyeew ahemfi no, na ɔmamfo no efiefi no, na wodwuruuw Jerusalɛm afasu no guu famu.
    9. Nna aweɔmfo safohen Nebuzaradan faa ɔman no nkaa a wɔkaa kurow no mu no; na hɔn a wɔdanee kɔr ne nkyɛn no so, na ɔman no nkaa a wɔkae no nyinara ndɔmmum kɔr Babilɔn.
    10. Na aweɔmfo safohen Nebuzaradan gyaa ɔman no mu ehiafo a wonnyi hwee no wɔ Juda asaase do, na ɔdze wenyin nture na mfuwa memaa hɔn da no ara.
    11. Afei Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar hyɛɛ aweɔmfo safohen Nebuzaradan wɔ Jeremia ho dɛ, JER.39.12, Fa no, na hwɛ no yie, na mma nnyɛ no bɔn biara; na dza ɔbɛse wo nyina yɛ ma no.
    12. Nna aweɔmfo safohen Nebuzaradan, na Nebusaziban, Rab-saris, na Nergal-sarezer, Rab-mag, na Babilɔnhen n'asafohen etsitsir no nyinara wɔsomae;
    13. wɔsomae ma wɔkɛfaa Jeremia fii aweɔmfo abangua no mu bae, na wɔdze no hyɛɛ Safan ba Ahikam ne ba Gedalia nsa, dɛ ɔmfa no nkɔ fie: nna ɔkɛtsenaa no nkorɔfo no mu.
    14. Afei Jeremia da ho da efiadze wɔ aweɔmfo abangua no no mu no, nna EWURADZE n'asɛm baa no hɔ dɛ, JER.39.16, Kɔ, na kɛse Etiopianyi Ebed-melek, dɛ, Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn no, ase nye yi: Hwɛ, mebɛma me nsɛm aba mu wɔ kurow yi do ayɛ mbusu, na nnyɛ papa bi a; na ɔbɛba mu wɔ w'enyim da no.
    15. Na da no mebɛgye wo, EWURADZE na ɔse: na wɔremmfa wo nnhyɛ mbarimba a isuro hɔn no nsa.
    16. Na nkwa na mebɛgye wo, na eronntɔ afona ano, na wo nkwa bɛyɛ afonam ama wo: osiandɛ ɔwo edze wo werɛ atwer me, EWURADZE na ɔse.

    Tsir 40

    1. Asɛm a ofi EWURADZE nkyɛn baa Jeremia hɔ, aber a aweɔmfo safohen Nebuzaradan gyaa no wɔ Rama n'ekyir no, ber a ɔfaa no dɛ ɔda nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn mu wɔ Jerusalɛm na Juda ndɔmmumfo a wɔdze hɔn rokɔ Babilɔn ndɔmmum no mu no.
    2. Na aweɔmfo safohen no faa Jeremia, na ɔsee no dɛ, EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn na ɔkaa mbusu yi baa bea yi do:
    3. na EWURADZE na ɔama aba mu, na ɔayɛ dɛ mbrɛ ɔkae no; osiandɛ hom ayɛ bɔn etsia EWURADZE, na hom enntsie ne ndze, dɛm ntsi na adze yi aba hom do yi.
    4. Na afei, hwɛ, Masan wo ndɛ da yi efi nkɔnsɔnkɔnsɔn a ɔda wo nsa no mu. Sɛ ehwɛ na oye ma wo dɛ enye me bɔkɔ Babilɔn a, bra, na mobɔhwɛ wo yie; na sɛ ehwɛ na omuo ma wo dɛ enye me bɔkɔ Babilɔn a, ma ɔnka: hwɛ, asaase no nyina da w'enyim; beebiara a ehwɛ a oye na ɔyɛ ahomka ma wo dɛ ebɔkɔ no, kɔ hɔ.
    5. Na onnyae nnsanee no, ɔsee dɛ, San mbɔ na kɔ Safan ba Ahikam ne ba Gedalia a Babilɔnhen ahyɛ no ambrado wɔ Juda nkurow do no, na kɛtsena ne nkyɛn wɔ ɔman no mu: anaa kɔ beebiara a ehwɛ a ibenya ahomka dɛ ebɔkɔ no. Nna aweɔmfo safohen no maa no akwantu mu edziban na ahyɛdze, na ogyaa no kwan.
    6. Nna Jeremia kɔr Ahikam ba Gedalia nkyɛn wɔ Mizpa, na ɔkɛtsenaa ne nkyɛn wɔ ɔman a wɔaka asaase no do no mu.
    7. Afei ber a dɔm no hɔn asafohen a wɔwɔ nhaban mu no, mekyerɛ hɔn na hɔn mbarimba no, wɔtsee dɛ Babilɔnhen ahyɛ Ahikam ba Gedalia ambrado wɔ asaase no do, na ɔdze mbarimba, na mbaa, na mbofraba, na asaase no do akɔhweaban a wɔammfa hɔn ndɔmmum annkɔ Babilɔn no mu bi ahyɛ n'ase no;
    8. nna wɔbaa Gedalia nkyɛn wɔ Mizpa, mekyerɛ Netania ba Ismael, na Karea mba Johanan na Jonatan, na Tanhumet ba Seraia, na Netofanyi Efai ne mba, na Maakanyi ne ba Jezania, hɔn na hɔn mbarimba.
    9. Na Safan ba Ahikam ne ba Gedalia kaa ntam kyerɛɛ hɔn na hɔn mbarimba no, dɛ, Mma hom nnsuro dɛ hom bɔsom Kaldeafo no: na hom ntsena asaase no do, na hom nsom Babilɔnhen no, na obesi hom yie.
    10. Emi dze, hwɛ, Mebɛtsena Mizpa megyina Kaldeafo a wɔbɛba hɛn nkyɛn no enyim: na hom dze, hom mboaboa nsa na ɔpɛber nduadzewa na ngo ano, na hom mfa ngugu hom ndzɛmba mu, na hom ntsenatsena hom nkurow a hom afefa no mu.
    11. Dɛmara so na Judafo a wɔwɔ Moab, na Ammonmba mu, na Edom, na hɔn a wɔwɔ asaase no nyina do nyinara, wɔtsee dɛ Babilɔnhen egya Juda nkaa, na dɛ ɔdze Safan ba Ahikam ne ba Gedalia edzi hɔn do ɔpanyin no;
    12. nna Judafo no nyina sanee fii mbea a wɔpaam hɔn kɔree no do bae, na wɔbaa Juda asaase do, wɔ Gedalia nkyɛn, wɔ Mizpa, na wɔboaboaa nsa na ɔpɛber nduadzewa piigyan ara ano.
    13. Nkyii so Karea na Johanan, na dɔm a wɔwɔ haban mu n'asafohen no, wɔbaa Gedalia nkyɛn wɔ Mizpa, JER.40.14, na wɔsee no dɛ, Ana inyim dɛ Ammonmba hɔn hen Baalis asoma Netania ba Ismael dɛ omboku wo? Na Ahikam ba Gedalia anngye hɔn enndzi.
    14. Nna Karea ba Johanan see Gedalia wɔ Mizpa wɔ nsumaa mu, dɛ, Meserɛ wo, ma monkɔ, na munkoku Netania ba Ismael, na nyimpa biara runnhu: ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na oboku wo, ma Judafo a wɔaboa ano aba wo nkyɛn no nyinara mbɔ mpetse, na Juda nkaa no nhera?
    15. Na Ahikam ba Gedalia see Karea ba Johanan, dɛ, Mma nnyɛ dɛm adze yi: na atorsɛm na eka no Ismael ho yi.

    Tsir 41

    1. Afei ɔbaa dɛ bosoom a otsia esuon no mu, Elisama ba Netania ne ba Ismael, a ofi ɔhen asefo, na ɔhen n'etsitsir no mu no, na mbarimba du a wɔka no ho no, baa Ahikam ba Gedalia nkyɛn wɔ Mizpa: na Mizpa hɔ na wɔbɔɔ mu dzidzii.
    2. Nna Netania ba Ismael, na mbarimba du a wɔka no ho no soɛree, na wɔdze afona twitwaa Safan ba Ahikam ne ba Gedalia, na wokum nyia Babilɔnhen hyɛɛ no ambrado wɔ asaase no do no.
    3. Ismael so kunkum Jewfo a wɔnye Gedalia wɔ Mizpa nyina, na Kaldeafo a wohun hɔn wɔ hɔ no, mbarimba akofo no a.
    4. Na ɔbaa dɛ oeku Gedalia ekyir ndaenu no a obiara nntsee no, JER.41.5, mbarimba bi eduowɔtwe fi Sekem, Siloh, na Samaria bae a woeyiyi hɔn abɔdwesa na woesunsuan hɔn ntar mu, na wɔatotow hɔnho akam, na edziban afɔr na nduhuam kitsakitsa hɔn nsamu, dɛ wɔdze reba EWURADZE fie.
    5. Na Netania ba Ismael fiir edzi fii Mizpa kehyiaa hɔn kwan, ɔrokɔ nyina nna orusu: na ɔbaa dɛ, ɔnye hɔn hyiae no, ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Hom mbra Ahikam ba Gedalia nkyɛn.
    6. Na ɔbaa dɛ, wɔbaa kurow no ne finimfin no, Netania ba Ismael, ɔnoara na mbarimba a wɔka no ho no kunkum hɔn, na wɔtoow hɔn guu mona no mu.
    7. Na hɔn mu mbarimba du see dɛ, Mma nnku hɛn: na yɛwɔ edzidzidze suma haban mu, ewifua na atoko, na ngo, na ewo. Nna ogyaae, na oennku hɔn ammfora hɔn nuanom no.
    8. Afei mona a Ismael toow hɔn a okunkum hɔn kaa Gedalia ho hɔn efun guu mu no, (ɔnoara nye dza ɔhen Asa tui wɔ Israelhen Baasha ho suro ntsi no) na Netania ba Ismael dze hɔn a wokunkum hɔn no hɔn efun hyɛɛ no ma.
    9. Nna Ismael faa ɔman nkaa a wɔwɔ Mizpa no nyinara kɔr ndɔmmum, mekyerɛ ɔhen ne mbabaa no, na nkorɔfo a wɔkaa Mizpa aweɔmfo safohen Nebuzaradan dze hyɛɛ Ahikam ba Gedalia n'ase no nyina Netania ba Ismael soaa hɔn ndɔmmum kɔree, na osii mu dɛ orukotwa mu akɔ Ammonmba no nkyɛn.
    10. Na Karea ba Johanan, na dɔm asafohemfo a wɔwɔ ne nkyɛn no nyina, wɔtsee mbusu nyina a Netania ba Ismael abɔ no, JER.41.12, nna wɔfaa mbarimba no nyina, na wɔkɔr dɛ wɔnye Netania ba Ismael rokɔko, na wɔkɔtoo no wɔ esu kɛse a ɔwɔ Gibeon no ho.
    11. Na ɔbaa dɛ nkorɔfo nyina a wɔwɔ Ismael nkyɛn no hun Karea ba Johanan, na dɔm asafohemfo nyina a wɔka no ho no, hɔn enyi gyee.
    12. Nna nkorɔfo a Ismael soaa hɔn ndɔmmum fii Mizpa kɔree no, wɔdandaan hɔnho, na wɔsensanee, na wɔkɔr Karea ba Johanan nkyɛn.
    13. Na Netania ba Ismael nye mbarimba baawɔtwe fii Karea nsa kɔr Ammonmba no nkyɛn.
    14. Nna Karea ba Johanan na dɔm no mu asafohemfo no nyina faa ɔman no nkaa no nyina a ɔkɛgyee hɔn fii Netania ba Ismael a okum Ahikam ba Gedalia wɔ Mizpa no nsamu no: mbarimba akofo, na mbaa, na mbofraba, na epiafo a ɔdze hɔn fi Gideon sanee bae no:
    15. na wosii mu kɔree, na wɔkɛtsenaa Gerut Kimham a ɔwɔ Bɛtlɛhɛm no, dɛ wɔnkɛhɛn Egypt, JER.41.18, wɔ Kaldeafo no ntsi: osiandɛ wosuroo hɔn, wɔ dɛ Netania ba Ismael eku Ahikam ba Gedalia a Babilɔnhen hyɛɛ no ambrado wɔ asaase no do ntsi.

    Tsir 42

    1. Nna dɔm no mu asafohen no nyinara na Karea ba Johanan, na Hosaia ba Jezania, na ɔman no nyinara, ofi ekumaba do kesi ɔkɛse do, twee bɛnee, JER.42.2, bɛsee nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia dɛ, Yɛserɛ wo, ma hɛn nkotoserɛ yi nsɔ w'enyi na yi EWURADZE, wo Nyankopɔn mpaa ma hɛn, nkaa yi nyinara; na hɛn nye kakraabi a yɛaka wɔ pii no mu, dɛ mbrɛ w'enyiwa tua hɛn yi:
    2. ama EWURADZE, wo Nyankopɔn aakyerɛ hɛn kwan kor a yɛnnantsew mu, na adze kor a yɛnyɛ.
    3. Nna nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia see hɔn dɛ, Matse hom asɛm: hwɛ, mibeyi EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn mpaa dɛ mbrɛ hom aka yi; na ɔbɛba dɛ asɛm biara a EWURADZE dze bobua hom no, mebɛpaa mu aka akyerɛ hom; mirinnsiw hom biribiara do.
    4. Nna wɔsee Jeremia dɛ, EWURADZE nyɛ nokwar dasefo turododo wɔ hɛn ntamu, sɛ yɛannyɛ dɛ mbrɛ asɛm nyina a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze bɔsoma wo wɔ hɛn nkyɛn no tse a.
    5. Sɛ oye o, sɛ omuo o, yebetsie EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn a yɛasoma wo ne nkyɛn no ndze: ama sɛ yetsie EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn ne ndze a oeesi hɛn yie.
    6. Na ɔbaa dɛ dadu soe ekyir no, EWURADZE n'asɛm baa nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia hɔ.
    7. Nna ɔfrɛɛ Karea ba Johanan, na dɔm no mu asafohen a wɔwɔ ne nkyɛn no nyina, na ɔman no nyinara, ofi ekumaba do kesi ɔkɛse do, JER.42.9, na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn a hom somaa me ne nkyɛn dɛ memfa hom nkotoserɛ nkɔto n'enyim no, ɔse nye yi:
    8. Sɛ hom bɛda ho atsena asaase yi do a, ɔnodze mibesi hom, na murunndwuruw hom nngu famu, na matsɛw hom, na menntutu hom ase: na menu moho wɔ mbusu a mabɔ hom no ntsi.
    9. Mma hom nnsuro Babilɔnhen a hom suro no no; mma hom nnsuro no, EWURADZE na ɔse: na mowɔ hom nkyɛn dɛ mebɛgye hom nkwa, na meyi hom efi ne nsamu.
    10. Na mibenya mbɔbɔrhu ama hom, na oehu hom mbɔbɔr, na ɔama hom asan akɔ homankasa hom asaase do.
    11. Na sɛ hom ka dɛ, Yɛrenntsena asaase yi do; ma dɛm no hom enntsie EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ne ndze;
    12. dɛ, Oho; na yɛbɔkɔ Egypt asaase do, mbrɛ yennkohu asayɛ, eso yɛnnkɛtse akasamu ne ndze, eso yennkedzi edzibankɔm; na yɛatsena hɔ a;
    13. ɔnodze afei, Juda nkaasefo, hom ntsie EWURADZE n'asɛm: mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE Israel Nyankopɔn no se nye yi, Sɛ hom dze si hom enyi do pɛpɛɛpɛ dɛ Egypt ara na hom bɔkɔ akɛyɛ amamforafo wɔ hɔ a:
    14. ɔnodze ɔbɛba dɛ, afona a hom suro no bɔto hom Egypt asaase do hɔ, na ɔkɔm a hom suro no betsiw hom dzendzenndzen wɔ Egypt hɔ; na hɔ na hom bowuwu.
    15. Dɛm na ɔbɛyɛ hɔn mbarimba nyinara a wɔdze esi hɔn enyi do pɛpɛɛpɛ dɛ Egypt ara na wɔbɔkɔ akɛyɛ amamforafo wɔ hɔ no nye yi; wobowuwu afona, na ɔkɔm, na ɔyardɔm ano: na hɔn mu biara rennka anaa oefi mbusu a medze bɛba hɔn do no mu.
    16. Na mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn no se nye yi: Dɛ mbrɛ m'ebufuw na m'ebufuhyew ehue egu Jerusalɛm mba do no, dɛmara so na, sɛ ekɛhɛn Egypt a, m'ebufuhyew bohue egu hom do: na hom bɛyɛ ekyiwadze, na ahobowdze, na ndom, na ahorohoraadze; na hom nnkohu bea yi bio.
    17. Juda nkaasefo, EWURADZE aka wɔ hom do dɛ, Mma hom nnkɔ Egypt: hom nhu no kotoo dɛ medzi hom dase ndɛ da yi.
    18. Na hom adaadaa homankasa hom akra; osiandɛ hom somaa me EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ne nkyɛn, dɛ, Yi EWURADZE, hɛn Nyankopɔn mpaa ma hɛn; na dza EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn bɛse nyina, dɛmara na ka kyerɛ hɛn, na yɛbɛyɛ:
    19. na ndɛ da yi mapaa mu aka akyerɛ hom; na hom enntsie EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ne ndze, wɔ dza ɔdze somaa me hom nkyɛn no mu biara mu.
    20. Dɛm ntsi afei hom nhu no ampaara dɛ hom bowuwu afona, ɔkɔm, na ɔyardɔm ano, wɔ bea a hom kɔn dɔ dɛ hom bɛyɛ hɔ amamforafo no mu.

    Tsir 43

    1. Na ɔbaa dɛ Jeremia kaa ɔman no nyina hɔn EWURADZE Nyankopɔn ne nsɛm a hɔn EWURADZE Nyankopɔn dze somaa no hɔn nkyɛn no nyina wiei no, mekyerɛ nsɛm yi nyina no, JER.43.2, Hosaia ba Azaria, na Karea ba Johanan, na ahopɔwfo no nyina kasaa kyerɛɛ Jeremia, dɛ, Eka atorsɛm: EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn no ɔnnsomaa wo dɛ bɛse dɛ, Mma hom nnkɔ Egypt nnkɛyɛ amamforafo wɔ hɔ;
    2. na Neria ba Baruk na opiapia wo tsia hɛn, ma oeyi hɛn ahyɛ Kaldeafo nsa, ma woeekuku hɛn, na wɔaasoa hɛn ndɔmmum akɔ Babilɔn.
    3. Na Karea ba Johanan, na dɔm no mu asafohemfo no nyina, na ɔman no nyina, woenntsie EWURADZE ne ndze dɛ wɔbɛtsena Juda asaase do.
    4. Na Karea ba Johanan, na dɔm no mu asafohen no nyina wɔfaa Juda nkaase nyina a wɔasan efi amanaman a wɔpaam hɔn kɔr hɔ nyina mu abɛyɛ amamforafo wɔ Juda;
    5. mbarimba, na mbaa, na mbofraba, na ɔhen ne mbabaa no, na nyimpa biara a aweɔmfo safohen Nebuzaradan daan no gyaa Safan ba Ahikam ne ba Gedalia ne nkyɛn no, na nkɔnhyɛnyi Jeremia, na Neria ba Baruk;
    6. na wɔbaa Egypt asaase do; na woenntsie EWURADZE ne ndze: na wɔbaa Tapanhes mpo.
    7. Nna EWURADZE n'asɛm baa Jeremia nkyɛn wɔ Tapanhes, dɛ, JER.43.9, Fa abo akɛse wɔ wo nsamu, na fa hyehyɛ ntaayaa nsɛwee a ɔwɔ Farao fie abowano wɔ Tapanhes no mu, wɔ Juda mbarimba no enyim;
    8. na se hɔn dɛ, Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn no se nye yi: Hwɛ, mobɔsoma akɛfa Babilɔnhen Nebukadenezar m'akowaa no, na medze n'akɔngua esi abo a medze ahyehyɛ ha yi do; na ɔaheran n'akatamanso do wɔ do.
    9. Na ɔbɛba abɔbɔ Egypt asaase; hɔn a wɔsɛ owu no, wobowu, na hɔn a wɔsɛ ndɔmmum kɔ no, wɔakɔ ndɔmmum, na hɔn a wɔsɛ afona no, afona aka hɔn.
    10. Na mobɔsɔ gya wɔ Egypt abosom efi mu, na ɔbɛhyew hɔn, na ɔasoa hɔn akɔ ndɔmmum: na ɔdze Egypt asaase bofura dɛ mbrɛ oguanhwɛfo dze n'atar hyɛ; na ofi hɔ befir edzi asomdwee mu.
    11. Obobu Bɛt-semes a ɔwɔ Egypt asaase do no n'edum no; na ɔdze gya ahyew Egypt abosom efi no nyina.

    Tsir 44

    1. Asɛm a ɔbaa Jeremia hɔ wɔ Jewfo nyina a wɔtse Egypt asaase do a wɔtsetse Migidɔl, na Tapanhes, na Nof, na Patros asaase do no ho, dɛ, JER.44.2, Mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE Israel Nyankopɔn no se nye yi: Hom ehu mbusu a medze maba Jerusalɛm do nyina, na Juda nkurow nyinara do; na, hwɛ, ndɛ da yi wɔayeyɛ amamfo, na nyimpa biara nntse do;
    2. osian hɔn emumuyɛ a wɔayɛ dze eyi me ebufuw ntsi, wɔ dɛ wɔkɔree kɛhyeew nduhuam, na wɔkɔsoom abosom afofor a hom nnyim hɔn ntsi, hɔn o, hom o, hom egyanom o.
    3. Naaso mosomaa mo nkowaa nkɔnhyɛfo no nyinara baa hom nkyɛn, mosoɛɛr ahema na mosomaa hɔn, dɛ, Ao, mma hom nnyɛ ekyiwadze a mikyir no.
    4. Na woenntsie, eso wɔammbrɛ hɔn aso adze dɛ wɔbɛsan efi hɔn emumuyɛ ho, dɛ wɔnnkɛhyew nduhuam ama abosom afofor.
    5. Dɛm ntsi na m'ebufuhyew na m'ebufuw huei gui, na ɔdzɛwee wɔ Juda nkurow na Jerusalɛm abrɔn mu; ma ayeyɛ ekurofo na amamfo, dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse ndɛ da yi.
    6. Dɛm ntsi afei mbrɛ EWURADZE, dɔm Nyankopɔn, Israel Nyankopɔn no se nye yi: Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na hom bɔ mbusu yi tsia homankasa hom akra, dɛ hom botwitwa hom mu ɔbarimba na ɔbaa, abɔdomaba na enumfoanoba efi Juda mu, dɛ mma wonngyaa hom nkaa bi;
    7. wɔ dɛ hom dze hom nsaano edwuma yi me ebufuw, dɛ hom rehyew nduhuam ama abosom afofor wɔ Egypt asaase a hom akɔ do akɛyɛ amamforafo wɔ hɔ no do; ama woeekuruw hom ase, na hom aayɛ ndom na ahorohoraadze wɔ asaase do amanaman nyinara mu?
    8. Ana hom werɛ efir hom egyanom emumuyɛ na Juda ahemfo emumuyɛ, na hɔn yernom emumuyɛ, homankasa hom emumuyɛ, na hom yernom emumuyɛ a wɔyɛɛ no Juda asaase do, na Jerusalɛm abrɔn no mu?
    9. Wɔmmbrɛɛ hɔnho adze ara dze bodu ndɛ da yi mpo, eso wonnsuroi, eso wɔnnantseew me mbra, anaa m'ahyɛdze a medze mesi hom enyim, na hom egyanom enyim.
    10. Dɛm ntsi mbrɛ dɔm EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn no se nye yi: Hwɛ, medze m'enyi bɛsa hom do, ma aayɛ hom mbusu, mekyerɛ dɛ wobokuruw Juda nyinara ase.
    11. Na mebɛfa Juda nkaase a wɔdze esi hɔn enyim dɛ wɔbɔkɔ Egypt asaase do akɛyɛ amamforafo wɔ hɔ no, na hɔn nyinara wɔasa: Egypt asaase do na wɔbɔtotɔ; wɔbɛhyew wɔ afona na ɔkɔm ano; wobowuwu, ofi ekumaba do kesi ɔkɛse do, wɔ afona na ɔkɔm ano: na wɔbɛyɛ ekyiwadze, na ahobowdze, na ndom, na ahorohoraa.
    12. Na mebɛtsea hɔn a wɔtse Egypt asaase do no, dɛ mbrɛ medze afona, ɔkɔm, na ɔyardɔm matsea Jerusalɛm no:
    13. na Juda nkaase a wɔkɔ Egypt aakɛyɛ hɔ amamforafo, no mu obi rimmfi nsa anaaso ɔnnka, dɛ wɔbɛsan aba Juda asaase a hom enya akɔndɔ dɛ hom bɛtsena do: na obiara rennsan, gyedɛ hɔn a wobefi nsa no.
    14.
